1936.12.16

Endon Returns to Luoyang from Shaanxi - Reports Chiang Kai-shek's Safety to Nanjing via Telegram - Endon Meets Chiang - Chiang's Demeanor Calm - Brief Conversation Without Discussing Political Issues - Chiang Believes Zhang's Proposals Are Not Worth Considering 1

(Nanjing) Endon and Huang Renlin flew from Luoyang to Xi'an on the 14th. At 5 PM on the 15th, Endon had already flown back to Luoyang from Xi'an and immediately made a long-distance phone call to President Kong's residence, reporting to Madame Chiang Kai-shek that after arriving in Xi'an, in addition to meeting with Zhang Xueliang, Zhang had also sent a staff member to guide him to meet with Chairman Chiang. Chiang's spirit was very good, his health was also sound, and he had absolutely no pessimistic attitude. The conversation time was very short, and no political issues were mentioned at all. The internal situation in Xi'an was not very clear, and so on. Currently, Endon is still staying in Luoyang. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Since the Xi'an Incident occurred, the people of the whole country have been very concerned about the safety of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Madame Chiang Kai-shek specifically requested the Englishman Endon to go to Xi'an to visit him. Endon arrived in Xi'an by plane from Luoyang at 12:30 PM on the 14th and immediately went with Zhang Xueliang and a translator to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. On the afternoon of the 15th, he took a plane back east. He originally planned to go directly to Nanjing, but due to heavy rain, he landed in Luoyang. He reported to Nanjing by long-distance telephone from Luoyang. It was reported that Chairman Chiang is currently residing in the residence of Division Commander Feng Qinzai, and his attitude is calm, as usual. Since the 12th, Zhang Xueliang has repeatedly visited, but Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has not spoken to him. This time Endon went to Shaanxi, and Zhang also accompanied him to pay his respects. Zhang repeatedly implored Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to adopt his proposals. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek told him that under the current circumstances, there was absolutely no room for consideration. Even if your opinions are beneficial to the entire country, you should also submit them to the central government for discussion. Endon told Chairman Chiang Kai-shek that Madame Chiang was extremely eager to come to Shaanxi to meet with him. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek said that there was no need to come to Shaanxi. It is heard that Madame Chiang Kai-shek plans to stay in Nanjing temporarily. It is also heard that Endon plans to fly from Luoyang to Xi'an again on the morning of the 16th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) The fact that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has still not regained his freedom is now regarded as certain here. Last night, it was rumored that Chiang is now under the protection of Yang Hucheng. After Endon took a plane from Luoyang to Xi'an, it has been more than twenty-four hours. Although it is heard that he has safely arrived in Xi'an, Endon himself has not sent a single word. Now everyone is looking forward to it. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Endon flew back to Luoyang on the 15th. In addition to reporting Chiang's safety to Madame Chiang Kai-shek by long-distance telephone, it is also heard that he sent telegrams to Kong Xiangxi, Ye Chucang, Chen Guofu, and Chen Lifu. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Yan Xishan will also send personnel to Shaanxi to persuade Zhang to escort Chairman Chiang back to the capital. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) This afternoon, after people here learned the news that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is still safe, they felt extremely relieved. Mr. Pan, an Australian advisor to Chiang, returned to Luoyang from Xi'an this afternoon and immediately made a long-distance phone call to Madame Chiang Kai-shek in the capital. It is said that he had met with Chiang in person, and Chiang's health was very good, and his spirit was also quite strong. Based on the above, it can be proven that the previous rumors that Yang Hucheng had revolted and pledged allegiance to the government were actually inaccurate. According to official news here, Mr. Pan only had a brief conversation with Chiang and did not discuss politics. After Madame Chiang learned the news of her husband's safety, she was extremely gratified. The government's opinion is that the fact that Chiang is still continuing to exist safely shows that Zhang Xueliang has complete control over the extremist elements in his army. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

Shao Yuanchong Struck by a Stray Bullet 2

(Nanjing) An official from Tongguan who came to the capital said that the news relayed by the road station was that Shao Yuanchong, a member of the Central Committee, was struck by a stray bullet from the mutinous soldiers in Lintong before noon on the 12th. The previous rumor about Qian Dajun was probably a misunderstanding. However, before anyone flies out of Xi'an, it is impossible to verify each other. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Certain Parties Pay Attention to the Evolution of the Shaanxi Incident 3

(Tianjin) According to a certain military department in Tianjin, if Zhang Xueliang [text missing] is not only a disaster for China but also a major concern for East Asia. A certain party has decided to devote all its efforts to paying attention to its evolution and to discuss response methods. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Ministry of Communications Orders Restoration of Shaanxi-Luoyang Telegraph - Tianjin-Shaanxi and Other Telegraphs Now Open 4

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications' radio between Luoyang and Xi'an, which had been disrupted and inaccessible since the Xi'an Incident, has been down for four days. It is now learned that the Ministry of Communications has ordered all relevant telegraph offices to quickly find ways to restore it. It is reported that the wired telegraphs will still take time due to pole and line issues. The wireless telegraphs are expected to be open for official and commercial telegrams on the 16th and 17th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) As of the 15th, ordinary mail to and from Xi'an has been restored. However, the post office said that it is being transferred via Zhengzhou, and parcels are still being refused. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) As of the 15th, Tianjin to Xi'an, both radio and wired telegraphs are open, but only commercial telegrams are allowed. It seems that the telegraph office in Xi'an is under the surveillance of the rebel army, and the sending and receiving are not free. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

No War in Xi'an City 5

(Nanjing) Fan Songfu sent a telegram stating that Xi'an is quiet and there are no signs of war in the city. Madame Chiang Kai-shek has received a telegram from Chiang reporting his safety. However, the telegram did not mention the situation in Xi'an. The city is still clearly chaotic. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

Longhai Express Train Runs to Tongguan 6

(Zhengzhou) The Longhai Railway's special express train No. 1 will be temporarily stopped in Zhengzhou from the 15th. Train No. 1 will depart from Zhengzhou East on the night of the 15th. Express trains Nos. 11 and 12 will run as usual to Tongguan. However, freight transport is slightly affected due to insufficient vehicles. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Zhengzhou) The western section of the Longhai Railway is damaged. From the 12th, westbound trains only sell tickets to Tongguan. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Tianjin Japanese Aircraft to Reconnoiter Xi'an 7

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Japanese military department will send aircraft to Xi'an to reconnoiter the situation there and the situation of Japanese residents. A certain staff officer will be sent. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Li Bai and Others Reply to Kong, Expressing Sorrow for the Shaanxi Incident - Guizhou Province is Now As Usual 8

(Guangzhou) Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, and Huang Xuchu replied to Acting President Kong, saying: "Dear Mr. Kong Yongzhi, Acting President in Nanjing, your message has been received. Chairman Chiang has been traveling around in recent years, without a moment to rest, and his loyalty to the country is well known to the world. Hanqing, deeply concerned about his homeland, was momentarily motivated by emotions and took action outside the bounds, causing Chairman Chiang to be stranded in Xi'an, shocking the whole country. I am especially saddened. I am grateful for your indication that the central government has already decided on the overall plan externally and is not alarmed by the temporary incident. Your mature strategy for the country is admirable. Everything here is stable as usual. Please ease your concerns. Respectfully replying, your younger brothers Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, and Huang Xuchu, kowtow in the cold." (14th) (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, and Huang Xuchu sent a telegram to Sun Ke on the 14th, stating briefly: "We are extremely shocked and saddened that Chairman Chiang suddenly encountered danger. The Suiyuan battle situation is still in a critical state, and now we have encountered this major change. The country's affairs will become more serious in the future. We earnestly hope that you, sir, and the central government officials will handle it properly and turn the crisis into safety. If we have any foolish ideas, we will present them at any time for consideration." (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

Overseas Consulates Inquire About Chiang's Safety 9

(Nanjing) After the Shaanxi Incident, overseas consulates have all telegraphed to inquire. They continue to receive telegrams from the Saigon Consulate stating: "Overseas Chinese are extremely concerned about the military mutiny in Shaanxi. Is it true? Please telegraph to indicate." The Rangoon Consulate telegraphed: "The Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is trapped in Xi'an, and overseas Chinese are extremely grieved. Whether he has escaped danger is especially hoped. Please telegraph quickly to indicate." The Bangkok Chamber of Commerce telegraphed, "We have heard that President Chiang is trapped in Xi'an. The entire overseas Chinese community is shocked. What are the facts? Please telegraph quickly to indicate." The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has replied to them separately, telling them that Chiang is now healthy. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Suma Visits Foreign Minister Zhang 10

(Nanjing) At 4:30 PM today, Consul General Suma visited Foreign Minister Zhang Qun at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to convey Ambassador Kawagoe's condolences after the Xi'an Incident and to hear information about the incident. (Allied News dispatch on the 15th)

Various Parties Request Punishment of Zhang One After Another 11

(Guangzhou) More than 5,000 representatives from various Guangdong civic groups, mass organizations, and schools held a general assembly of all sectors to condemn Zhang and quell the rebellion on the 15th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Zhengzhou) The Special Party Headquarters of the Longhai Railway sent a telegram to all sectors of the country on the 14th, unanimously advocating submitting a request to the central government to punish Zhang Xueliang. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Hankou) The Hubei Journalists Association, various theater associations in Hankou, the Wuhan Literary Society, the Jianghan Thinking Tide Society, and the Zhongxing Weekly sent a telegram to the central government on the 14th, requesting a clear order to punish Zhang. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Chongqing) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Farmers' Association, the Municipal Education Association, the Municipal Newspaper Association, and the Municipal Workers' Club here recently jointly telegraphed the central government, requesting severe punishment for Zhang Xueliang. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Kunming) Long Yun and Xue Yue sent a special telegram to the central government and a telegram to the whole country on the 14th, denouncing Zhang Xueliang. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

(Zhengzhou) The Zhengzhou Longhai Party Headquarters, the County Party Headquarters, the Chamber of Commerce, and the Journalists Association are extremely indignant at Zhang Xueliang's betrayal of the party and the country and his coercion of the commander-in-chief. They sent a telegram to the whole country, unanimously denouncing him. The Zheng Office of the Northwest Bandit Suppression Headquarters was disarmed at noon on the 14th. (Special dispatch on the 5th)

The Capital Announces Martial Law 12

(Nanjing) The Nanjing Garrison Headquarters received an order to announce martial law from the 16th and to inform the citizens. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Wuhu) Representatives from all circles in Wuhu gathered at the Xinhua Theater on the morning of the 15th to hold a general assembly. Commissioner Gao Wenbo reported on the government's handling of the Shaanxi Incident and telegraphed the central government, vowing to be the government's backup. A telegram was sent to Xi'an urging Zhang to escort Chairman Chiang back to the south. In order to stabilize the locality, the Special Commissioner's Office implemented martial law from the 15th, investigating and arresting treacherous people who spread rumors and issuing announcements to stabilize prices. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Ma Hongkui, Liu Zhenhua, and Others Telegraph the Central Government Expressing Support 13

(Nanjing) Ma Hongkui, Chairman of Ningxia Province, Liu Zhenhua, Chairman of Anhui Province, Division Commander Mao Bingwen, Hu Zongnan, Zeng Wanzhong, Guan Linzheng, Fan Hanjie, Ding Delong, Zhou Xiangchu, Kong Lingxun, Li Jilan, Wang Yaowu, Wang Wenyan, Tao Zhiyue, Li Ying, Tang Huaiyuan, etc., Han Fuqu, the Third Route Commander, and Division Commander Sun Tongxuan, etc., as well as the heads of the security offices of Zhejiang and Henan provinces, etc., have telegraphed the central government and the National Government regarding Zhang Xueliang's rebellion, expressing their support for the central government and requesting an order to punish him. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Xue Yue telegraphed Kong Xiangxi on the 14th, stating briefly: "Chairman Chiang's life is tied to the survival of the country and the nation. In recent years, he has led the masses and devoted himself to the cause of domestic pacification and resistance to foreign aggression. All those with blood and qi love and support him. However, Zhang Xueliang dared to raise troops to coerce and hold him, acting as an accomplice to foreign invaders, directly seeking to destroy our country and nation. My hatred is extreme. I swear to protect the central government and rescue the leader with my head and hot blood and not share the same sky with Zhang the traitor." (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Ma Hongkui, Chairman of Ningxia, was extremely indignant after receiving a telegram from the central government informing him that Zhang Xueliang had rebelled in Xi'an and coerced the commander-in-chief. On the morning of the 15th, he flew to Zhengzhou from Ningxia with his entourage and will go to Luoyang. Whether he will come to the capital is currently undecided. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Changsha) The Student Self-Government Association expressed to He their support for the central government and their determination not to be incited by external forces. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Beiping) Zhang Zuoxiang, the former governor of Jilin Province, currently stationed in Tianjin, stated today that he is willing to support the central government and denounce Zhang Xueliang. Wan Fulin, who is staying in Baoding, also announced his loyalty to the government this morning, saying that he and his subordinates will continue to be under the command of Song Zheyuan. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

Rumor that Zuo Yi Telegraphs the Central Government - His Attitude of Defending the Territory and Resisting Aggression is Firm - A Large Number of Puppet Troops Continuously Arrive in Shangdu - The Bandits and Puppets Plan to Take Advantage of the Opportunity to Launch a General Offensive Against Suiyuan East 14

(Guihua) After the Shaanxi Incident occurred, it is rumored that Zuo Yi formally telegraphed the central government on the 15th, expressing his position. His attitude of defending the territory and resisting aggression is firm. Enemy planes bombed the territory of Taolin and Xinghe in Suiyuan East. On the 15th, enemy planes dropped many bombs in Damiaozi, Wulanhua, and other places in Suiyuan North. Zeng Yanyi returned to Suiyuan from Niao Lanhua on the 15th to visit Fu and report on the situation in Suiyuan North. On the afternoon of the 15th, Fu Zuoyi and Zhao Chengzhou convened a meeting of senior generals such as Sun Changsheng. Sun Ding returned to Suiyuan North for defense that night. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Guihua) The puppet troops added to the defense of Shangdu have reached more than 3,000. The puppet troops originally garrisoned at Jiabusi have all been transferred to Shangdu. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Guihua) Prince De has arrived in Shangdu from Jiabusi. The number of puppet troops increased in Shangdu is about one division. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) A telegram from Jining stated that the bandits and puppets plan to launch a general offensive against Suiyuan East. On the 13th, Prince De led Zhuo Shihaibao Yueqing and various Mongolian puppet troops to Shangdu and Kangbao. On the 14th, they had already harassed our Jiuguquan Hongmaoyinger and the side of Xinghe with cavalry. There were also formations of aircraft dropping bombs. Dozens of trucks were sending troops to the front. Fu Zuoyi returned to the province from the front on the 14th. After receiving information from all sides, he was deeply saddened, but still gathered the generals with tears in his eyes, vowing to follow Chairman Chiang's policy. During this critical period, he will carefully prepare the front defense and not allow the bandits and puppets to take advantage of the opportunity. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) A telegram from Jining stated that the chief of a certain party's special agency stationed in Jiabusi flew to Chang on the 13th to discuss plans to take advantage of the opportunity to harass. Currently, military supplies between Dolun are being increased to Suiyuan East in large quantities. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) A certain party outside the Pass has finalized its military plan for Suiyuan, which is to launch a general offensive against Bailingmiao Damiao. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) A telegram from Jining stated that Tang Enbo encouraged the soldiers at the front on the 14th, urging them not to be dispirited because Chiang was coerced and held, but to continue to follow Chairman Chiang's policy to resist and annihilate the enemy. The soldiers all wept and shouted that they would swear to protect the central government and obey military orders. Therefore, the morale of the front is still strong. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Qingdao Japanese Marines Withdraw Part of Their Troops to Their Ships - The Remaining Troops are Scheduled to Return to Their Ships Today - The Order in Various Cotton Mills is Good 15

(Qingdao) On the 15th, the number of workers who went to the cotton mills was slightly higher than on the 14th, and the order was good. The ground has returned to normal. The marines of the Japanese warships Nagara and Kumano withdrew first on the 15th. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Qingdao) A total of more than 300 Japanese marines were withdrawn on the 15th. The remaining troops are scheduled to return to their ships gradually from the 16th. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Page 4

Cheng Qian and Others Advise Zhang Xueliang - Heads of Universities in Peiping Advise Zhang to Withdraw from the Brink 16

(Nanjing) Cheng Qian, Chief of the General Staff Headquarters, Tang Shengzhi, Director of Training, Zhu Peide, Director of the Office of the Military Affairs Commission, and others telegraphed Zhang Xueliang and Yang Hucheng in Xi'an on the 14th, urging them to wake up and protect Chairman Chiang and come out to save the country. The original telegram is copied below: "To Mr. Zhang Xueliang and Mr. Yang Hucheng in Xi'an, we have received your telegram of the 12th. We are extremely astonished at the rebellion of the Northeast Army. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek bears the heavy responsibility of the country's safety. For more than ten years, he has been secretly planning for resisting aggression and seeking survival, working tirelessly day and night. The facts are obvious and need no further explanation. Since the unification of the country, people's hearts have become more united, and morale has become more inspired. The central government's attitude towards foreign countries has become more active, and international opinion has changed. We were saying that from national unity and concerted efforts to move forward, it is not difficult to wipe out the shame of lost territories. However, just as the Suiyuan war was in full swing, there was a sudden act of coercing the commander-in-chief, rebelling against superiors and creating chaos, and betraying the party and the country. Its crime is really billions of times greater than that of traitors and those who sell out the country. Those who are close to them are hurt, and those who are enemies are pleased. No one with a human heart would do this. Your advocacy of tolerance towards the Communists may be a deception. You should also suggest that the central government hold a meeting to discuss so that the national policy can be decided by public opinion and the steps will not be divergent. Why do you take this worst policy and give the enemy a chance to attack? Now, for your sake, the only thing to do is to immediately support Chairman Chiang and come out to save the country, then this difference in thought can still be forgiven. If you are obsessed and do not wake up, you will be ruined and discredited. It will be too late to regret it in the future." Signed: Cheng Qian, Tang Shengzhi, Zhu Peide, Yang Jie. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Li Liejun, a member of the Central Committee, telegraphed Zhang Xueliang and Yang Hucheng on the 15th, urging them to wake up. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Peiping) After the sudden outbreak of the Shaanxi Incident, educational circles here were shocked upon hearing the news. The heads of various universities in Peiping, Jiang Menglin, Mei Yiqi, Xu Songming, Li Zheng, Li Shuhua, Lu Zhiwei, and Li Lin, etc., telegraphed Zhang Xueliang on the 15th, advising him to immediately withdraw from the brink, protect Chairman Chiang Kai-shek from danger, and surrender to await punishment. The original text reads: "To Mr. Zhang Hanqing in Xi'an, the Shaanxi Incident has shocked the whole country. Mr. Chiang bears the heavy responsibility of the country. If he is harmed, the country's cause will be regressed by at least twenty years. You should remember the national disaster and family feud, withdraw from the brink, protect Mr. Chiang from danger, and surrender to await punishment, or you may still be able to redeem yourself to the people of the country. If you are obsessed and do not wake up, your name will be deeply appreciated by the enemy, and you will forever be the sinner of the country and the nation." (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Two hundred and seventy-five young generals from all over the country, Hu Zongnan, Huang Jie, Li Mo'an, Sun Yuanliang, Li Yannian, Yu Jishi, He Zhonghan, Deng Wenyi, Mao Bangchu, etc., recently sent a telegram to Zhang Xueliang to advise him to restore Chairman Chiang's freedom. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 14th)

(Nanjing) Wang Bailing telegraphed Zhang Xueliang on the 15th, asking him to stop at the edge of a cliff. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Hong Kong) One hundred and seventy organizations, including the Hong Kong Overseas Chinese Education Association, the South China Film Association, and the Hong Kong and Kowloon Chinese Workers' Union, telegraphed Zhang Xueliang on the 15th, urging him to quickly protect Chairman Chiang and return to the capital. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Qingdao) Peng, Xu Wenguo, Gu Gengye, and others from the Northeast fellow villagers' film industry in Qingdao, a total of 1,532 people, telegraphed Zhang Xueliang on the 14th, asking him to accompany Chairman Chiang to leave Shaanxi for the capital as soon as possible to discuss national affairs together. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanjing) Hua Qiao Ze Mo Sun, Chen Ji and others from British, Dutch, Siamese, Japanese and French territories, who recently returned to the country, were extremely indignant at Zhang Xueliang's act of rebellion and coerced the commander-in-chief. On the 15th, they jointly telegraphed Zhang, advising him to pull back from the precipice and escort Chiang Kai-shek back to Beijing with all speed. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

(Tianjin) Famous personalities out of office in Tianjin will send a general telegram advising Zhang to quickly repent and not to fall into the path of destruction. The telegram is being drafted and will be sent out within days. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Tianjin - The Market is Calm 17

(Tianjin) On the 15th, all sectors in Tianjin were waiting for news of Chiang's safety. The market was generally calm. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Nanchang) People here are indignant about the Shaanxi situation and are calling for a clear order to punish the rebels. Concrete measures have been taken. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Yan Xishan Replies to Zhang Yang's Telegram, Questioning Four Issues 18

(Yangqu) After the Xi'an Incident, Zhang Xueliang and Yang Hucheng jointly telegraphed Yan, reporting on the incident. Yan replied to Zhang and Yang by telegram on the 14th, saying: "I have carefully read both your telegrams and Mr. Zhang Hanqing's original telegram. I am extremely shocked and saddened. I have four questions to ask you: First, how will you handle the aftermath? Second, will your actions increase the strength of resistance or decrease it? Third, will you shift the civil war to a war against foreign aggression, or will you shift the war against foreign aggression to a civil war? Fourth, can you guarantee that it will not develop into an extremely tragic massacre in the country? Previously, in Luoyang, Mr. Han once said with tears that he believed that Mr. Chiang had the determination to save the country, but there were contradictions in his methods. Now, are you using the enthusiasm to save the country to carry out actions that endanger the country? I remember advising Mr. Han that today the country is in extreme danger, and disagreements will ultimately harm the country and should be pursued slowly. Disagreements are not good for the country. Now your actions are abrupt, increasing the worries of the people of the country. I am infinitely saddened for the country, for the nation, and for you. Please understand and take care of yourselves." Signed: Yan Xishan. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

(Beiping) A reporter passed through Suiyuan and returned to Peiping. On the 14th, he visited Yan Xishan at the Suiyuan Commissioner's Office. Yan told the reporter that he was fortunate that domestic unification was taking place and the Suiyuan war was coming to a small conclusion. He did not expect to suddenly receive a telegram about the Xi'an Incident on the evening of the 12th. The shocking news was so alarming that he was even more shocked. The greatest pain in his life, apart from his father's death, was this. At this time of national crisis, it is still difficult to cope with the combined strength of the whole country. If another civil war breaks out, can it not lead to a tragic bloodshed, deepen the degree of foreign aggression, and reduce the strength against foreign countries? This is a matter of great importance to the survival of the country. He earnestly hoped that Chairman Chiang would be rescued first and that the incident would be resolved peacefully as soon as possible in order to save the country together. He had telegraphed Zhang Xueliang on the 14th to advise him tactfully, asking him what he intended to do about the aftermath. He said that he had stopped the civil war. Is this action promoting the civil war? He said that he was united against foreign countries. Is this preventing the war against foreign countries? There are only two paths for all countries in the world. Which path should our country take? The country and the nation should be the premise. The entire nation should stand on one line of defense. It must not be divided and disintegrated. Otherwise, in future world wars, anyone who fails will be sacrificed by our compatriots. The misery is unimaginable. In this Suiyuan war, it was very painful to see that the dead on the enemy's side were all Chinese compatriots. He bears the responsibility of defending the territory of Jin and Sui, and he is determined to fulfill his duty not to lose an inch of land. He will listen to the central government's orders for national policy. If it is beneficial to the country and the nation, he will not hesitate to make any sacrifices. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

National Press Declaration on the Current Situation: Support All Domestic and Foreign Policies of the Government; Only President Chiang is the Pillar of the Nation and the Leader of the Country 35

(Nanjing) The national press is indignant at the Xi'an rebellion. On the previous two days, it initiated and published a "Joint Declaration of the National Press on the Current Situation" to express its views on the current situation. During the two days, newspapers from various places sent telegrams to express their support. As of tonight (the 15th), the newspapers that have signed their names have spread throughout the country. The domestic opinion circles, with newspapers and news agencies from all over the country unanimously linked, have issued a joint declaration, which is still a first in Chinese press history. Its expression of opinions has had a significant impact and can be imagined. The original text is recorded as follows:

On the fourth day that Military Affairs Commission Chairman and Executive Yuan President Chiang Kai-shek was in distress in Xi'an, the national press, with the joint signature of various newspapers, publicly expresses its common views on the current situation, hoping that all circles at home and abroad will listen attentively. First, China's current situation is one in which internal troubles and external aggression are intertwined and multiplied, and the issue of survival is at stake. In this situation, if we want to seek the independence and survival of the country, we must ensure the independent and autonomous position of everything internal and external, and gather the thoughts and talents of the people of the country to make the greatest efforts under one direction. During this period, the entire country should absolutely adhere to this unchanging attitude towards any event or problem, and should also absolutely take the survival of the nation-state as the highest basis for any doctrine or thought. Firmly adhering to this attitude, we believe that the national policy and administrative policy of the National Government in the past few years are just in line with this standard, and are indeed sufficient to guarantee the survival of our nation. The national disaster has been brewing for five years, and those who plot against us cannot harm our national life, national spirit, and material construction, but have instead made considerable progress. The reason for this is precisely because the government's position is serious and firm, and the government's policy is completely connected with public opinion. Based on the facts of the past few years, we firmly believe that if we want to maintain the life of the country and complete the revitalization of the nation, we must absolutely support the National Government and support all the government's domestic and foreign policies. All people of the country who have a sense of national and national consciousness should share our views and beliefs. The way to dedicate oneself to the country today is to exert one's strength in one's position to assist the government, consolidate order, and maintain the overall situation.

Second, in the past hundred years, various organizations and forces in our country have repeatedly been on the verge of collapse, and our international position has been reduced to that of a colony. In the face of numerous national disasters, the country has changed its appearance, and foreign invaders have been rampant. In this time of hardship, difficulty, and turmoil, who is it who has worked hard and loyally to establish a center of gravity for the country and to strengthen the strength of the central government? Who is it who has rectified national defense and built the people's livelihood? Who is it who has changed customs and disciplines? In other words, who is it who has enabled our 400 million compatriots to become organized from having no organization, to have a country from having no country, to save the compatriots from fire and water, and to put the people on the path to prosperity? The answer is, only President Chiang is the pillar of the nation and the leader of the country. He is entrusted with the lives of 400 million people and the master of 5,000 years of history. Who in the universe is plotting to harm this leader? Who is the common enemy of 400 million people? In our conscience, Zhang Xueliang, even if he is a villain, would not dare to harm a single hair of the leader, as it is a natural law. Today, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's military power is the heart of 400 million people, and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's background is the 5,000-year history of the nation. Zhang Xueliang, the rebel leader in Xi'an, is now defying the great injustices of the world. Even if he is as vicious as a jackal, his heart may still reveal a moment of conscience. Today, we are calling on the national public opinion to strictly supervise Zhang Xueliang's conscience, and we are mobilizing the historical pens of all Chinese and foreign reporters to reserve the final verdict on Zhang Xueliang's merits and demerits for thousands of years to come, urging him to restore the Chairman's freedom and safety immediately, and escort him out of the country, so that the national leader can continue to lead his work of saving the nation and revitalizing it.

Third, there is righteousness in heaven and earth, and there are disciplines in the country. The more difficult the times are, the more urgent the changes in the world are, and the ways to solve and deal with them should be simpler and clearer. The righteousness of heaven and earth and the disciplines of the country are the only guidelines for correcting chaos and returning to order in our national history, and they are also the only guidelines for suppressing chaos and resolving difficulties today. What is the central organization of the country today? What is the guidance system of the government? It is in the teachings of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the creator of the Republic of China, and the spirit of his successors. It is also in the party that guides the government. Although the current situation is extremely complicated, the government's position must adhere to a fixed and correct attitude, respecting the history and legal system. Moreover, what Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has held in the past few years to lead the whole country and maintain the upper and lower levels is to inherit the teachings of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, that is, to uphold righteousness and maintain discipline. This spirit is the life of the leader, and we should cherish this spirit as much as we cherish the life of the leader. Righteousness and evil cannot coexist, and righteousness and evil cannot stand together. We firmly believe that the national public opinion will be able to give play to its spirit and strength and be the backing of the government to suppress chaos and pacify the rebellion. We must also believe that the national public opinion and the strict formation of the people's will are sufficient to sweep away various "false and eloquent" and "seemingly right but actually wrong" claims, and to eliminate all "vacillating" and "misleading" thoughts. This is not a high-profile "or empty talk, but the natural law for pacifying chaos and determining change today. At this time of war and rapid changes, the situation is turbulent and heartbreaking. Dare to take the responsibility of public opinion, list the humble opinions, contribute to the government, and point out to the people. The enthusiasm of the patriotic people to suppress chaos and determine change will inevitably be ardent, and the will to protect the survival of the nation will inevitably be firm. With this sincerity and loyalty, and by urging the government and awakening the people, we will surely be able to overcome great difficulties and turn danger into safety. We once again sincerely pray for the safety of the leader and look forward to the return of the leader. European Travel Correspondence

The Distance Between Peoples (1) 37

— Xu Yu

In Bombay, we visited almost every place, we saw special shops, we saw Indians who were much thinner than the Shanghai Indian patrol, and we also saw a lot of Indian historical culture in the museum. But my understanding of India, at least for me, did not come from these sights as much as it did from the conversations and observations of the group of young Indian people who boarded the ship in Bombay to study in Europe. In the museum, what surprised me the most was Indian painting and musical instruments. I didn't remember the dates recorded on them, but anyway, in those very early times, their painting and musical instruments had already reached a considerable stage of development, and Chinese painting and music of the same period seemed to be far inferior to them. Yet, such a nation is now looked down upon by everyone, and the Chinese are also looking down on them.

After that group of Indian students boarded the ship, the crowd of people seeing them off on the dock seemed to be seeing us off as well, and we inadvertently waved our hands at them. The ship had set sail from Shanghai at four in the morning. The people who saw us off all went back by one or two o'clock. The Chinese students, tired from the past few days, fell asleep at that time, and when they woke up it was already seven or eight o'clock. The ship was already floating in the sea, surrounded by vastness, with no relatives in sight—so they felt infinite envy for that group of Indian students who were able to pull paper and wave to their relatives and friends who were seeing them off. Indians have more intense facial expressions than Chinese when they talk, and their emotions are more exposed than those of Chinese. The loud laughter of many young women in the crowd seeing them off seemed to be something that Chinese people didn't have. I thought at the time that it was a very meaningful thing for that group of several educated young Indians to be companions with dozens of Chinese young people on this white ship for more than ten days, and to interact with the Chinese youth with their naked emotions. Although it was not a friendly meeting of any form, at least it was a contact between two ethnic groups, and there could be some mutual understanding. But in fact, it wasn't like that!

Indians have many "uncivilized" (?) habits, walking on the deck in their pajamas, often squatting on the toilet with dirty feet to relieve themselves, and a certain smell in the room. At the dining table, they sometimes put used toothpicks back into the toothpick holder. All kinds of dirty and casual behavior soon made the Chinese look down on them and dislike them. Once they were disliked, they naturally didn't want to get close to them again.

However, I understand these bad habits of theirs. Every nation has bad habits, but the aspects they are manifested in are different. These bad habits of Indians are very common in inland China, especially in the border areas. Students in universities who have been Westernized for a long time may have shed their backward habits, but I think, in everyone's hometown, are many compatriots still living with many bad habits? Those are our elders, our brothers and sisters, do we also look down on them like this? In Europe, I am now in Paris, and I don't think they have many good habits either. For example, early in the morning, walking on a small street, residents on the third or fourth floor would beat blankets, shake bed sheets, and brush clothes over your head. Is this a matter of public virtue? I feel that public virtue is not morality, it is just a habit. Habits exist in every aspect. For example, when eating, we northerners think it is strange when we first see Cantonese eating snakes, but in fact, people who eat snakes would think it is strange not to eat snakes. When Westerners arrive in China, they scold China for all kinds of unhygienic habits; if shaking bed sheets from the window was a Chinese habit, what would Westerners say the first time they encountered it, saying that the Chinese are a nation that does not value public virtue at all! Now there is no need to say that Cantonese eating snakes is barbaric, and there is no need to look down on someone just because they have certain bad habits; naturally, we may as well bring each other to good habits. In the inland areas, I saw many Western Catholic priests wearing Chinese cloth robes, jackets, cloth shoes, and cloth socks, living with so-called all kinds of bad habits. I also know that Mr. Wu Zhihui said in his lecture that Mr. Chen Duxiu's son deserved to die, saying that he was a communist, saying that he was extremely dirty, that he didn't wash his face for several days, that he never brushed his teeth, and that he ate extremely dirty things with workers and rickshaw pullers; (Mr. Wu's eloquence, as well as the lecture records, are definitely better than mine, and the original manuscript cannot be found now, so I only remember a rough outline.) I am not a Catholic, nor am I a communist, but in addition to the love and respect for this spirit, I also consider that the real approach and understanding between two people, two classes, and two nations requires humbly and calmly overcoming these habit distances.

The distance between peoples is not just a matter of habits. Language and writing are also something we cannot ignore; however, language and writing are a kind of barrier, which everyone knows and cannot be crossed for a while. However, we and the Indians have already communicated through English in this regard. But because of the distance of habits, the most outstanding members of these two groups of people, during more than ten days on the same boat, most of them did not exchange a word; I think this is a very unfortunate thing.

In fact, there is a distance not only between peoples, but also between people. Not counting the opposition between groups, in daily life between individuals, are we all putting on faces and maintaining insurmountable distances? - Especially in cities, neighbors of ten years may not exchange a word, people on the same streetcar every day for five years may not greet each other, and people who eat at the same table every day all year round may not say a word, making this lively world so lonely. What kind of animals are humans after all?

In Shanghai, when I lived in Hongkou, I met a maid leading three children to school on the streetcar every day. One was twelve years old, and the younger ones were seven or eight years old. Another boy was probably only six years old. Sometimes they came back on the same streetcar. I had been seeing them often for three or four months. One day when I was going home, those three children also got on the streetcar halfway. Maybe there was something going on at home, or there was a guest, or the maid had quit her job. Anyway, that day there was no one to accompany them. The older girl was carrying a schoolbag in one hand and leading her little brother with the other. The little girl was carrying two book bags that seemed big. After coming up, this little girl had a very hard time coming up. I helped her a little at that time. They didn't show anything, so when I was about to get off the streetcar, because I knew the alley (hutong) where her house was, which I passed every day, I said, "I'll carry your schoolbags for you." But to my surprise, the older girl stared at me and said, "What do you want to do?" And everyone on the streetcar was paying attention to me. This attention was a bit contemptuous, not saying that I was tricking her out of her schoolbag... (To be continued)

Current Affairs Commentary

A Perspective on Schacht's "Territorial Expansion Theory" 38

— Xing

German Minister of Economics Schacht recently gave a speech at a memorial meeting in Frankfurt, the general idea of which was that the allocation of colonies is the only way to solve the current world problems. At present, Germany does not have sufficient land to supply the necessary raw materials and food, so it cannot guarantee the safety of Germany's existence. And if Germany wants to achieve world peace, territorial expansion is also an important step. The implication is that Germany has the right to demand a redistribution from other countries because the supply of raw materials and food is insufficient. This tone is not only a full exposure of the founding spirit of Fascist Germany, but also shows that Germany's economy has reached a dead end due to the rearmament.

Everyone knows that Germany's international credit has greatly declined since the financial crisis in 1931. Because of the heated market competition, the trade surplus has also shrunk year by year. Under such circumstances, if Germany wants to absorb huge amounts of military raw materials and food from abroad in a short period of time to complete its military preparations, it will have to create irreparable scars on its finances. The facts show that Germany's gold reserves and foreign exchange each had 804 million and 114 million marks at the beginning of 1933, but at the end of October, the total gold reserves and foreign exchange were only 70 million marks. Although there has been a trade surplus of about 600 million marks in the past three and a half years, Germany has also used "exchange agreements" to purchase goods from various countries on credit. These raw materials and food purchased on credit are stipulated in the contract that the payment will only be made after a long period of time after import. Therefore, the foreign currency exchanged for German exports has to be mostly used to repay old debts. In other words, most of the military preparations that Germany has completed so far still have to rely on the continued production and export of industrial products in the future to repay its costs.

From this, we can know that Germany's rearmament has only increased the future external burdens of the German production sector, which is obviously a fatal blow to German finances. Germany's gold and foreign exchange have long been very empty. If the mark depreciates, it will only increase the debt. If it does not depreciate, although German debt can benefit from the debt reduction due to the currency depreciation of creditors, German goods will inevitably encounter serious setbacks in the international market due to higher prices. As a result, the military preparation plan will be shaken.

In the past four years, Germany's rearmament has been smooth sailing. The main reason is that countries in Southeastern Europe and Central Europe have supplied Germany with large quantities of raw materials and food. Now the situation is somewhat different. First, in the past, countries in Southeastern Europe and Central Europe were willing to lend to Germany despite the risk of funds being blocked because Germany could buy at higher prices. Now, world prices have risen uniformly, and the number of countries buying raw materials and food is increasing day by day. Countries in Southeastern Europe and Central Europe do not have to rely solely on German sales. Second, Germany's economy is becoming more and more deteriorated. The exchange agreements established between various countries and Germany are now gradually being terminated. Especially after the agreement between the United Kingdom, the United States, and France, this trend is even more obvious. Due to the above two reasons, it is certainly not as easy for Germany to continue to purchase raw materials and food in the world market in the future as it was before.

In short, Germany's isolation in the world economy in the future is very obvious. If she does not stop the plan to expand its military preparations, then she can only resort to war.

Pan-American Conference, Japan Pays Unusual Attention, Deeply Afraid of Weakening Its Existing Position in South America, Japan's Far Eastern Policy Will Also Be Affected 39

(Washington) The Japanese diplomatic community is paying very close attention to the Pan-American Peace Conference currently being held in Argentina, because what is being discussed at the conference may have a great impact on Japan's position in South America. In recent years, Japan's commerce in South America has been a major enemy of the United States, and it has greatly encouraged immigration to South America, so it is paying special attention to commerce and immigration. Experts believe that if the American countries establish a neutrality agreement, Japan will also be affected, because the US Congress has recognized that the American countries have considerable common relations with belligerent countries outside the Americas, and they will never recognize the land conquered by force. Therefore, it also has implications for Japan's Far Eastern policy. (National Telegram on the 14th)

Cuban Senate Passes New Draft Constitution 41

Equitable Distribution of Landed Property, Labor Nationalized

Cuban Capital The Senate today passed a new draft constitution, which includes provisions for requisitioning private property and strengthening social security. The land of large landowners will be distributed equally, and labor will also be nationalized. British Foreign Secretary Eden Speaks Out, Calls for World Peace, Armistice on Armaments to Promote Economic Cooperation, Opposes Formation of Opposing Groups, Anglo-French Mutual Assistance Should Not Be Seen as an Alliance 42

(London) British Foreign Secretary Eden gave a speech in Bradford today, calling on the world to stop the arms race and engage in economic cooperation. The main points of Eden's speech are as follows:

If the people of the world want to enjoy lasting peace, they must reform certain trends that are currently manipulating world politics. Today, the world's wealth is being used too much for military preparations. If countries insist on rearming, the result will be economic exhaustion. If we can abandon the arms race and engage in economic cooperation instead, then its wisdom will be beyond our reach. We British are extremely willing to see the realization of this change and are prepared to do our best to promote it. Our efforts to make the Tripartite Monetary Agreement a success are one example, because we believe that if we act according to this agreement, progress will be visible. We urge all countries to follow suit so that the international economic situation can become brighter, and there can be greater opportunities for prosperity and hope between countries, and that the living standards of the people of the world can be improved as a result. If all the difficulties in the world, an arms agreement, and a permanent solution are obtained, then we British are also willing to wholeheartedly help its success. If countries need economic or financial assistance from the United Kingdom in order to increase their military preparations, we will resolutely reject them, because the result will cause a great threat to world peace.

Eden then briefly outlined the general principles of British foreign policy, saying, "We will reject any dangerous doctrine of dictators who are biased towards the left and right wings. The United Kingdom's cooperation with others is not based on the form of a government, but entirely on whether it is willing to maintain peace with its neighbors and whether it can abide by treaty obligations. It must be known that when there are conflicts of opinion between countries, if treaty obligations can be respected and preparations for free negotiations can be made at any time, then international trust can be maintained permanently, and there must be considerable restrictions on the unilateral abolition of various treaties.

Eden also expressed his welcome to the declaration made by French Foreign Minister Delbos the other day, saying that if the United Kingdom and Belgium are invaded for no reason, the entire French army will automatically be used for the defense of the United Kingdom and Belgium, but he strongly denied that the above declaration and his own declaration in Lemington on November 20 contained the intention of concluding any special alliance or promoting an alliance policy, and said that the above two guarantees were only used to deal with the situation created after Germany abolished the Locarno Treaty and sent troops to the demilitarized zone. The British and French governments not only have no intention of establishing special measures, but are also quite willing for Germany to join in cooperation to jointly handle the affairs of the entire Europe. In short, we do not want any alliances and fortresses to exist within Europe.

Eden also recalled in the official statement in Lemington the degree of need for British military preparations, because there are significant British interests all over the world, and in order to give them full protection, there must be considerable military preparations. Therefore, he believes that making a clear announcement is enough to help world peace and leave no room for doubt in the minds of the world. Eden continued, "Today's world has shrunk much more than before, and because of the increasing development of science, the world is even smaller. Therefore, if there are any changes in any part of the world, our interests are in danger of being affected. We should pay close attention to it at all times and in all places, and we must not neglect it because it does not concern us. For the above reasons, I have repeatedly stated that my country's foreign policy, because the country has numerous and broad interests, must go towards broad solutions. If it is not like this, the peace and trust that we hope for will be difficult to achieve." (Reuters Telegram on the 14th)

Dispute Between Turkey and France Over the Issue of Ethnic Minorities in Syria, Turkish Foreign Minister Explains His Position, French Representative Replies 43

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations held an open meeting this afternoon to discuss the issue of Turkish ethnic minorities in the cities of Alexandretta and Antioch in Syria. Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü stated his country's views and requested the Council to consider the following three items separately: (1) In terms of the current status of the Turkish ethnic group in the two cities of Alexandretta and Antioch, it is necessary to take several transitional measures. The Council should be asked to make a decision. (2) The basic points of the dispute over the Turkish ethnic group issue in the two cities. (3) A statement that the friendship between France and Turkey is profound and will not be affected by temporary disputes. Rüştü first explained the Turkish government's position from the perspective of law and economics, and then refuted France's view that this issue is a dispute between Turkey and the League of Nations. He also said that the Turkish population in the two cities of Alexandretta and Antioch has always accounted for the majority, so the Turkish government requested the Council to conduct an objective study of this issue in order to seek a normal and appropriate solution so that the local area can be peaceful and the rule of law can be respected. Before the dispute is resolved, the League of Nations should control the fate of the two cities and order the French troops stationed in the two cities to withdraw completely, replacing them with a small number of neutral police forces, and a special commissioner appointed by the League of Nations will command them. After Rüştü finished speaking, the French representative, Deputy Foreign Minister Viénot, immediately stood up and expressed his gratitude for Rüştü's statement on the friendship between France and Turkey, and stated that he would reply to the main points of the dispute on this issue tomorrow. The Council then appointed Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler as the rapporteur for this case at the proposal of Viénot, and scheduled to continue the meeting at 11:00 a.m. tomorrow so that Viénot could attend and state France's views. (Havas Telegram on the 14th)

(Geneva) At 11:30 this morning, the Council of the League of Nations continued to discuss the issue of Turkish ethnic minorities in the cities of Alexandretta and Antioch in Syria. French Deputy Foreign Minister Viénot gave a speech to explain his country's views in order to reply to the claims made by Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü yesterday. He said that Syria and Lebanon are both places entrusted to France by the League of Nations. According to the League of Nations Covenant, the ruling country must be responsible for guaranteeing the territorial integrity of the entrusted territory. Although the original resolution adopted by the League of Nations can be changed, if the claims made by Turkey regarding the ethnic minorities in the above two cities are implemented, the future will definitely have the most serious impact, because the above two cities have been incorporated into the Syrian territory for fourteen years. If they are divided in the future, causing the independent sovereignty of Syria to be reduced, then the Arab ethnic group in Syria will violently resist, which can be asserted. However, France is still willing to take various measures in each of the cities to prevent border disputes or other accidents. For example, the League of Nations appointing neutral observers to inspect the area can also be accepted by France. (Havas Telegram on the 15th)

(Geneva) The rapporteur on the issue of ethnic minorities in Syria, namely Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler, recently invited representatives from France and Turkey after the Council meeting to study the transitional measures he could propose (i.e., the measures to be taken before the dispute is resolved). The representatives from France and Turkey immediately agreed to send neutral observers to each of the cities. The French representative also agreed to withdraw the reinforcements sent to Antioch when riots occurred previously, but did not agree to withdraw all the original troops stationed in each of the cities and replace them with neutral police forces, because this measure is tantamount to abandoning the rights of the ruling country. Regarding this, the Turkish representative insisted on the claims he made at the Council meeting yesterday and said that if he could not obtain satisfaction, he would give up his right to vote when the Council votes on the transitional measures. (Havas News Agency Telegram on the 15th)

(Geneva) Regarding the dispute between France and Turkey, it is heard that international figures here have drafted a solution, one of the most notable of which is to follow the precedent of the Åland Islands after the European War and establish the same system in each of the cities. (The Åland Islands are in the Baltic Sea and belonged to Sweden before the European War. It was not until after the European War that they were changed to Finland, and their neutral status was guaranteed by various countries.) According to the current treaty between France and Syria, it is stipulated that each of the cities should be under the protection of the League of Nations and guaranteed by Syria. If a new system is adopted in the future, an additional guarantee will be added. (Havas Telegram on the 15th)

Labour Leader Snell and the Archbishop of Canterbury both rose to express their support for the response. The wording of the responses from both houses was the same, the gist being that both houses should pledge allegiance to the Emperor and the Queen, and that the Emperor's reign would surely protect the freedom of the country and promote the prosperity and well-being of the people, it is said. Madrid Suburbs Rebel Attacks Fail Sending Fresh Troops to the Front German Volunteers Participate in Combat 55

Madrid The Nationalist forces recently launched offensives in the Guadarrama Mountains north of the capital, the town of Boadilla to the southwest, and the town of Valdemorillo to the south, but were repelled by government forces and suffered heavy losses. In the Boadilla area, the Moroccan troops belonging to the Nationalist forces and the German volunteers who recently arrived at the front to assist in the battle launched particularly fierce attacks, using aircraft and many tanks as cover. The two sides fought for five hours, and as a result, the rebel army was completely defeated, abandoning more than two hundred corpses and suffering numerous injuries. In addition, aircraft belonging to the government forces flew to the Garaitagort railroad station in the province of Aragon in the northeast and bombed it effectively. There were no battles on other fronts. (Havas, 15th)

Navalcarnero (in the hands of the Nationalist forces) The weather has been bad in the Madrid area recently, and aircraft must fly at low altitudes of 300 meters to advance, so air force activity has been completely suspended. As of now, the foreign troops are the main force in the Nationalist forces fighting on the front line. These troops have been fighting for a long time and are inevitably exhausted. The Nationalist authorities here are now sending fresh troops to assist in the battle. It is estimated that the total strength of the Nationalist forces is no less than 500,000 men, of which 100,000 men are Carlist troops and volunteers. Members of the Spanish Falange mostly participate in military training in the rear, and are not as numerous as the Carlists in practice. The Nationalist authorities are gradually sending new recruits to the front lines, so there are traces of them on all fronts. In addition to those in the vicinity of Madrid, on other fronts such as Asturias in the northwest and Aragon in the northeast, the defense lines held by new recruits are often as long as 100 kilometers. Professor Newmen, an ear specialist, and another neurologist were specially summoned to the castle today to treat him. However, those who have seen the Duke feel that his complexion is very good, obviously different from before he abdicated. The Duke got up at 9 o'clock this morning, had breakfast alone, and then answered telegrams. It is said that the Duke's wedding with Mrs. Simpson will be very simple, with only a few close friends invited to attend. (National Telegram, 14th)

(Vienna) The Duke of Windsor, the former British Emperor now living in Enzesfeld as a guest of Baron Rothschild, is resting in his bedroom due to a slight cold. It is heard that the former Emperor has rented a house in Kitzbühel from an American millionaire. (Reuters, 15th)

Under the Japanese Plan: Five-Year Industrial Development of the Northeast, Raising 1.5 Billion Yuan to Promote the Work, Actively Preparing for a Wartime Economic System 73

Changchun Correspondence: The Japanese have finalized the general outline for the five-year plan for industrial development in the Northeast and will begin its implementation next year. The framework of the industrial five-year plan is based on heavy industry, agriculture, animal husbandry, forestry, transportation, water management, civil engineering, and other sectors as the core for development. It also aims to revitalize existing related enterprises. The necessary development funds for the plan total 1.5 billion yuan, and the fundraising methods are as follows: (1) The puppet organization will issue domestic and foreign bonds of 600 million yuan; (2) The South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) will invest 200 million yuan; (3) The Japanese Ministry of Civilian Affairs will invest 400 million yuan; (4) The puppet Manchurian Industrial Bank will issue bonds of 200 million yuan. The main entities for development are: (1) The puppet government and special corporations; (2) Mantetsu and its affiliated agencies; (3) Free enterprise agencies relying on Japanese private investment; (4) New enterprise agencies relying on the puppet Manchurian Industrial Bank. According to the intentions expressed by the Japanese side, Japan and the puppet state will establish a comprehensive economic system and prepare for the formation of a wartime economic system, thereby implementing a new stage of industrial policy. Given the current international pressing situation, the establishment of a so-called "Japan-puppet as one" economic system is an absolute necessity. According to the focus of the five-year plan, in terms of the structure of Japanese capitalism, it prepares the Northeast economy for the transition to a wartime system, aiming to complete Japan's sole control and national policy from the traditional role of the Northeast as a raw material supply base. Such as the iron and steel national policy, aviation national policy, fuel national policy, power control, etc. The scope of the areas expressed in this new industrial plan is as follows: (1) Increased coal production; (2) Increased pig iron production; (3) Coal liquefaction plan; (4) Hydropower generation; (5) Laying of the fourth new railway line; (6) Promotion of water management projects; (7) Development of agricultural, animal husbandry, and forestry products; (8) Development of military industry; (9) Promotion of various existing industries accompanying these projects. Regarding the five-year agricultural plan, in all aspects, the Japanese intend to move away from the soybean-centered monoculture system and gradually transition to a diversified agricultural system. To clearly express the main crops targeted for increased production under this agricultural policy, such as wheat, rice, oats, barley, flax, hemp, ramie, cotton, tobacco, sugar beets, soybeans, food crops, sorghum, millet, corn, etc., reaching more than ten varieties. In the first year of the plan, the total amount of subsidies for increasing the production of these agricultural products is 3 million yuan, with the details as follows:

Wheat

Among the 3 million yuan wheat production increase subsidy, 1.2 million yuan is allocated for wheat. Considering it as a target for industrial development, and considering the relationship between North Manchuria and wheat cultivation in the current stage of Northeast agricultural production, the Japanese side states that self-sufficiency in food raw materials is an urgent task for achieving national policy.

Flax Cultivation

Flax is a new special product of the Northeast, and the Japanese regard it as promising. They plan to implement full-scale subsidies starting next year. They have already planned to purchase 540 kilograms in areas such as Liaoyang, Liaozhong, Shenyang, Haicheng, Yingkou, Gaiping, Fuxian, Xinmin, Tai'an, and Jin County. Starting next year, the flax sowing area will be 250 mu. In addition, the current cultivated area of flax is 14,000 mu. The Japanese believe that the demand for flax in the Northeast is increasing year by year, with high import volumes. Aiming to meet the needs of both Japan and the puppet state for flax, the cultivated area will be increased by 5,000 mu next year, totaling 20,000 mu. The current central company for flax production, Man-Nichi Flax Co., Ltd., will actively promote flax consignment planting.

Tobacco

The cultivation of American yellow tobacco in the Northeast has traditionally been centered in Fengcheng and has been quite developed. However, due to poor weather this year, the harvest is only 700,000 kwan, an increase of 20% compared to last year. The Japanese consider the accounting for tobacco cultivation to be quite good and plan to promote full-scale production increases in the Fengcheng area, along the Anfeng Railway line, and in various parts of the puppet Jinzhou Province starting next year, recognizing it as one of the promising industrial targets.

Grains

Rice, oats, sorghum, millet, corn, etc., under the production increase plan, aim to achieve self-sufficiency for both Japan and the puppet state.

Animal Husbandry

Considering the suitability of the Northeast climate and environment, the Japanese plan to establish a livestock production increase plan, maintain excellent breeding stock, and promote and improve livestock breeding, which is greatly needed by both Japan and the puppet state.

Cotton

A new stage of cotton promotion in South Manchuria has been delineated. This year, the cultivated area increased by 60% compared to the previous year, with a harvest of twice the yield. The commissioned seed cultivation area is 1,300 cho, with a total harvest of 1.73 million catties. Next year, there is an expansion plan for the commissioned seed cultivation area to 5,500 cho. Furthermore, due to the Japanese's active promotion, farmers are induced to cultivate more cotton.

Other

In addition, the Japanese are also promoting special-purpose crops such as perilla, peanuts, and sesame seeds, shifting from a single-crop farming system to a multi-crop farming system. This shift is one of the cornerstones of the five-year industrial plan.
