Arrangements by the Hebei-Chahar Authorities to Cope with the Situation: Convening a Meeting of Mayors and Officials from Both Provinces, Telegraphing Zhang Xueliang to Rein in at the Brink, Admonishing Students in Various Schools to Avoid Agitation 75

Beiping Correspondence: After news of the Xi'an Incident arrived in Beiping, the authorities and the diplomatic corps expressed deep concern and attention. On the 12th, the British and Japanese embassies in China both held meetings. The British side decided to await the true details of the incident, while the Japanese side happened to coincide with the inspection of troops in Tianjin by the Japanese Army Commander stationed in Tianjin, Tashiro Wan'ichiro, who remained in Beiping. Starting at 9 PM, he convened a meeting at the Japanese embassy with foreign and military personnel, as well as representatives of Japanese residents, to discuss everything until 3 AM on the 13th. They decided to maintain a wait-and-see attitude. When the highest authorities here first received the news, they only learned that 40-50 li of the western section of the Longhai Railway had been destroyed, assuming it was a mutiny. It was not until after 3 AM on the 13th that they received further news of Zhang Xueliang's rebellion, which was very surprising. They also received a telegram from He Yingqin, learning the details of the incident. Song Zheyuan, Chairman of the Political Affairs Committee, then convened a meeting at 9 AM on the 13th at his private residence in Wuyiku Hutong, inviting military and political officials Qin Dechun, Feng Zhi'an, Shao Wenkai, Chen Jiyan, Lei Sishang, etc., to discuss everything. Jia Deyao, Tang Yulin, etc., were also present. The discussion lasted until around 11 AM, and it was decided to make efforts to maintain law and order. Furthermore, due to many rumors in Beiping after the Xi'an Incident, the Public Security Bureau issued a special order on the afternoon of the 13th, strictly prohibiting the spreading of rumors to prevent unscrupulous individuals from instigating unrest. Therefore, the situation in the streets remained as usual. It is reported that Chairman Song told visitors that he was shocked by the confinement of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and believed that in this time of national hardship, this extraordinary change was a national misfortune. He also believed that this matter was Zhang Xueliang making a huge mistake by being surrounded by the Communist Party. Chairman Song's attitude was extremely calm, and he took the protection of local security as his responsibility, implementing strict precautions. He also telegraphed Minister He Yingqin with this intention, stating that he would only follow the orders of the Central Government in all other matters.

After the Xi'an Incident occurred, the Hebei-Chahar authorities immediately telegraphed the mayors and officials of the two provinces of Hebei and Chahar to come to Beiping to discuss everything. Feng Zhi'an, Chairman of Hebei Province, had already arrived in Beiping, and Zhang Zizhong, Mayor of Tianjin, also arrived soon after. Liu Ruming, Chairman of Chahar Province, also arrived in Beiping from Zhangjiakou at 7 AM on the 14th. At 10 AM, Song Zheyuan went to Nanyuan after paying respects to Duan Qirui and addressed the officers above the rank of battalion commander. Feng Zhi'an, Zhang Zizhong, Liu Ruming, Qin Dechun, Ge Dingyuan, Fu Zhankui, etc., also accompanied him. In addition to reporting the situation in their respective areas to Song, they also consulted on everything. They returned to the city around 4 PM. Feng and others returned to their posts separately within the day to earnestly maintain law and order. At 6 PM in the evening, Song telegraphed Kong Xiangxi and He Yingqin, saying, "We are shocked to hear of the situation in Shaanxi. The Communist Party harms the country and the people. To save the country, we must first suppress the Communists. Hanqing (Zhang Xueliang) has been used by the Communist bandits to instigate disturbances, which is heartbreaking to the entire nation. We should request the Central Government to quickly quell the rebellion, rescue Chairman Chiang, and implement the established policy of suppressing the Communists to maintain the foundation of the nation. Zheyuan respectfully leads his subordinates and awaits orders on the frontier. If it benefits the country, we will not hesitate. We pray that you will issue instructions at any time so that we may follow them." At the same time, he also telegraphed Zhang Xueliang, asking him to prioritize national affairs, rein in at the brink, and especially ensure the safety of Chairman Chiang. The telegram was extremely earnest. After the telegram was sent, no reply had been received as of 3 AM on the 15th. Furthermore, telegraphic communications between Beiping and Shaanxi had not been restored, so the true situation in Xi'an could not be ascertained.

The Beiping city area remained calm as usual. The Public Security Bureau, as a preventive measure, issued an order to strictly investigate household registrations and investigate the activities of Communist Party members from that day onwards to reassure the people. Teachers and students in various schools held meetings, and many students held separate symposiums to study and analyze the incident. School principals held a luncheon meeting on the afternoon of the 14th, attended by Li Zheng, Xu Songtao, Lu Zhiwei, Jiang Menglin, Mei Yiqi, Hu Shi, etc., who exchanged opinions on current affairs for a long time. As a result, they all believed that at a time when China's international standing was gradually increasing, the country should unite to face external challenges and should not have other problems. It was decided that the authorities of various universities would jointly telegraph Zhang Xueliang to advise him.

Furthermore, after receiving a telegram from Minister of Education Wang Shijie, instructing them to do their best to prevent student agitation, the Beiping city authorities were immediately invited by Mayor Qin Dechun to meet with the presidents of various universities at the city government at 4:30 PM on the 14th. In addition to reporting the recent situation, he also hoped that the presidents of the various universities would assist the Beiping city authorities in maintaining order within the schools and ensuring that they remained calm and stable. The meeting ended at 5:30 PM. Regarding middle schools, the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Lei Sishang, convened a meeting with the principals, hoping that the principals would do their best to control the internal affairs of the schools under the current circumstances, avoid agitation, maintain a calm spirit of attending classes in individual environments, and connect well in terms of organizations to achieve a unified effect. (15th)

Martial Law in Wuhan After the Xi'an Incident, Solidified Law and Order, Field Headquarters Hastily Established, Provincial Government Reorganized Immediately, Zhang Yang Telegrams He Chengjun, Actually Asking to Fly to Shaanxi to Consult 76

Hankou Correspondence: The Xi'an Incident occurred, shaking the entire nation. Wuhan is the hub connecting north and south and occupies an important strategic position. However, high-level military and political institutions are in a period of reorganization. Not only military and political affairs must be accelerated, but local order should also be vigorously maintained. Regarding political aspects, the highest institution is the Hubei Provincial Government. Although acting Chairman Lu Zhu is responsible for maintaining the status quo, it is unknown when the newly appointed Chairman Huang Shao-hong will arrive. All members of the Provincial Government telegraphed Huang to urge him to come. Huang was originally scheduled to travel west on the 15th, but now it has been slightly delayed due to certain matters. He is expected to arrive in Hubei by plane around the 20th to take office. As for the heads of the various departments, it is rumored that there will be changes in the Construction and Education Departments, while the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments will remain unchanged. The Secretary-General needs to be replaced as Lu Zhu has been transferred elsewhere. Regarding military aspects, the highest institution was formerly the Pacification Commissioner's Office for Hubei, now the Wuhan Field Headquarters. He Chengjun was previously ordered to close the Commissioner's Office and cease operations, while the Field Headquarters was planned to be established on New Year's Day. However, the Xi'an Incident happened to occur at a time when the Commissioner's Office had already been abolished but the Field Headquarters had not yet been organized. In order to facilitate issuing orders and responding to emergencies, He Chengjun specially advanced the establishment of the Field Headquarters to the 13th, still operating at the Commissioner's Office and borrowing the Commissioner's Office seal. He will move to Wuchang on New Year's Day. On the evening of the 12th, He convened all senior officers at the former site of the Commissioner's Office to discuss ways to consolidate law and order. The next day, he issued a martial law order in the name of the Director of the Field Headquarters. Guo Chan, the Wuhan Garrison Commander, announced his compliance that evening. On the same day, He Chengjun led 28 generals, including Xu Yuanquan, to telegraph the Central Government, expressing their sincere support for the established national policy and standing by ready for orders.

Qingdao: All Japanese Textile Mills Resume Work, Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus Send Personnel to Assist, Japanese Marines Retreat to Ships After Work Resumes 77

Qingdao Correspondence: The labor strikes at various Japanese textile mills in Qingdao have been resolved through negotiations with the city authorities. The mills have decided to resume work uniformly on the 14th. On the one hand, the Sifang Office, together with the Public Security Bureau, convened a meeting of village and town chiefs, ordering them to instruct workers to work at the mills with peace of mind. On the other hand, Dong Zhidao, section chief of the Social Affairs Bureau, led personnel to inspect various textile mills and informed them of the following six key points: (1) Workers requested to be dismissed and expelled from various factories, those from outside the city shall be sent back to their hometowns by the Public Security Bureau; those originally from the city shall be guaranteed and monitored by their village chiefs; (2) If any dismissed workers return to the city, or if there are still bad workers after work resumes, the Social Affairs Bureau can be notified for investigation; (3) If any unscrupulous individuals prevent workers from going to work before or after work resumes, the patrol team of the Public Security Bureau will investigate; (4) If disputes arise after work resumes, the Social Affairs Bureau must be notified at that time so that personnel can be sent to handle them at any time; (5) Matters, large or small, shall be handled cooperatively; (6) The method of notifying workers to go to work, in addition to the announcement by the city government, those in the city have already been ordered by the Social Affairs Bureau's director to the offices in various rural areas to quickly convene village and town chiefs to notify workers to go to work. At the request of the factories, the Social Affairs Bureau has telegraphed the county governments to notify the workers to comply. To ensure that workers can work with peace of mind, the Social Affairs Bureau has formulated measures to station factory personnel in various textile mills to mediate labor-management misunderstandings in case of incidents. The Public Security Bureau has also formulated temporary measures to deal with the resumption of work to maintain order. On the morning of the 14th, all factories resumed work simultaneously. The Social Affairs and Public Security Bureaus and the Sifang Office all sent personnel to the factories to assist in handling matters. The number of workers resuming work in each factory, according to the proportion of the original number of people, is more than 70%. The workers who resumed work are also working with peace of mind, and the situation is very good. As for the withdrawal of the Japanese Marines, the Japanese side stated that they had decided to withdraw to the ships after work resumed. The number of workers resuming work in each factory on the 14th and the measures for the Social Affairs and Public Security Bureaus to send personnel to the factories and handle the resumption of work are recorded separately below.

Number of Workers Resuming Work in Each Factory:

Measures for the Social Affairs Bureau to Station Personnel in Factories: (1) Send one person to each factory to monitor the resumption of work by workers in shifts A and B at 5 AM on the 14th; (2) In case of labor-management misunderstandings or disputes, the stationed personnel shall request instructions for handling at any time; (3) After the workers go to work, the factory shall report the work situation to the stationed personnel at any time for investigation and verification. If there are any bad workers, they will be dealt with together with the Public Security Bureau after being reported by the factory; (4) If the factory encounters difficulties after work resumes, the stationed personnel shall report and request instructions for handling at any time; (5) The stationed personnel shall report the work situation, the number of male and female workers on duty, and work efficiency on a daily basis; (6) The stationed personnel shall not propose measures or casually talk with workers regarding workers' work matters without authorization; (7) The stationed personnel's meal expenses shall be paid by this bureau; (8) The stationed personnel shall go to the factory for inspection together with the factory personnel; (9) The stationed personnel shall not leave the factory without orders.

Measures for the Public Security Bureau to Handle the Resumption of Work: (1) Number of police: In addition to the original officers and police of the Sifang Cangkuo Branch, the Public Security Bureau shall send Inspector Zhu Fu to lead two squadrons, one squadron stationed in Sifang, one squadron in Cangkuo (partially stationed in —Shuiqinggou), and send Inspectors Chong Jisheng and Huang Jicheng to be stationed in Sifang and Cangkuo to handle everything; (2) Overtime dates: Starting from the 13th, patrol separately in the Sifang Cangkuo area and guard the designated places to perform duties. Withdraw appropriately depending on the situation after work resumes; (3) Duty allocation: One police squad shall be stationed in front of each factory gate to take turns on duty. The entire squad shall work overtime when workers go on and off duty. A total of nine squads of police should be dispatched for nine factories. The remaining police shall be responsible for patrol matters; (4) Patrol routes: Sifang is divided into five sections, and Cangkuo is divided into four sections. One police squad shall be assigned to each of the above patrol sections. In addition to the full mobilization from 5:00 to 7:00 in the morning and evening (when workers go on and off duty) to patrol each section in rotation, they should also patrol each section once every two hours. (December 14th)

Songjiang 79

County Magistrate Digs Up and Burns Rice Roots

In order to prevent the breeding of rice borers next spring, which would be harmful to rice and cotton, the county government ordered all districts to instruct township and bao-jia chiefs to urge farmers to flood their fields with clear water when the weather is cold, so that they would freeze and ice, causing the borer eggs to freeze to death at a certain temperature, or to dig up the rice roots, pile them up and burn them, to destroy the borer eggs. Now, repeated orders have been issued, listing this as the main task of the township and bao-jia chiefs. Each bao must dig up at least 10,000 catties of rice roots and designate them for stacking and disposal to be burned after the district inspects them according to regulations.

Kunshan 80

Poison Eradication Campaign Propaganda

The county's Poison Eradication Campaign Conference and Health Campaign were held jointly at the sports field at 9:00 AM on the 15th. More than 3,000 people participated, chaired by County Magistrate Peng Baichuan, who led the ceremony. Then, the significance of the meeting was reported, followed by speeches by representatives of various agencies. Finally, slogans were shouted and a parade was held before dispersing. In the afternoon, groups set out to give lectures and distribute a large number of publicity materials to raise awareness.

Boy Scouts Raise Funds to Aid Sui

The campaign to aid Sui in all circles of the county is extremely enthusiastic. Recently, the Boy Scouts have also formulated fundraising measures to comfort the soldiers at the front: Boy Scout troops will save petty expenses to be used as donations for comfort, and troops will take turns holding donation tubes to solicit donations from tourists.

Nanhui 81

Intercept Male and Female Bandits

When a bus that has always operated between Shanghai and Datuan and Xin Ji'an arrived at Xin Chang Town on the 12th, several well-dressed passengers disembarked, including a woman who was particularly fashionably dressed, and her actions were very suspicious. They were detained by the patrolling guards. When the woman saw the men being detained, she ran west in a panic. She was instructed to call the Shangtuan in Xiasha Town and asked them to send members to intercept her. A box gun and a pistol were found on her, and the bullets were already loaded. She was sent to Xin Chang for investigation and was sent to the county Public Security Bureau for interrogation on the 13th. It is reported that the arrested bandits were named Lu Arong, Shen Jinwen, Wang Xitong, and the woman was named Shi Lanying. Their purpose in coming to the south seemed to be robbery.

Jiading 82

Two Robbery Cases Solved Together

After the home of the late County Councilor Zhu Kentang outside the West Gate of Naxi Township, Yaxing Temple, was robbed of gold jewelry worth hundreds of silver dollars last month, the home of Bu Xusheng was robbed of more than 300 silver dollars in jewelry and cash on the night of the 10th of this month. The robbed items in both cases were obtained during the day, and the bandits came that night, indicating that the bandits were locals. Zhang Bin, a detective from the County Public Security Bureau, immediately started an investigation and obtained a lead, first arresting Zhu Pingao, nicknamed Yeji Amao, in Dujiacun near his residence, and then arresting Li Amao and two others in Lijiacun. After strict interrogation, they confessed to their crimes and also confessed that Peng Xinquan and others lived in Yaxing Temple. They then went to arrest Peng, whose father, Peng Zhongchang, was the local bao chief and had already reported the case to the county government.

Wuxi 83

Cotton Yarn and Rice Prices Soar

After the Xi'an Incident occurred, it had a great impact on all parties. There have been many changes in the business community in the past two days. On the 14th, the market prices of rice, cotton yarn, and rice all rose. Cotton yarn rose by two yuan per piece, and rice rose by one or two jiao per dan. In addition, the price of paper increased unabated, with newsprint at six yuan per ream, white offset at four yuan, 50-pound kraft paper at eleven yuan, colored kraft paper at nine yuan and eight jiao, and drawing paper at two jiao and five fen per pound. Furthermore, items such as flour, cloth, and foreign goods have also soared in price, making it difficult for the poor to make a living.

Discuss Local Security

The county government convened a joint meeting of representatives from party, government, military, police, and legal organizations at 9:00 AM on the 15th to discuss measures to maintain local security. More than 90 people attended, chaired by County Magistrate Long. He reported that the county's defense should be arranged properly and that he had ordered the subordinate public security organs to comply. Then, Zang Qifang, the administrative inspector of the second district, reported on Zhang Xueliang's rebellion. Finally, Li Tiban, Qian Sunqing, Hou Baosan, and others expressed their opinions before the meeting adjourned.

Coal Panic in Various Factories

Due to transportation issues, coal supplies for various silk, yarn, and flour factories in the county have been scarce recently, causing panic. The county chamber of commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Railways, requesting permission to allocate vehicles specifically for transporting coal. Yesterday, it was learned that the coal companies in Wuxi have little coal in stock, and since the Xi'an Incident, the Longhai and coastal railways have been disrupted by military activity, making it even more difficult to transport coal, cutting off supplies. Various counties have become panicked. Fan Yulin, the director of the Qijianyan Silk Factory, made a special trip to Nanjing yesterday to report to the National Government's Construction Committee, but he has not received coal assistance.

Dangtu 84

Two Robbery Cases Occur in the Vicinity

The home of Xue Shugeng in Suoqiaowan, outside the West Gate of Wuyi, is located in a bustling area. Unexpectedly, at about 2:00 AM on the 14th, seven or eight bandits suddenly arrived, each carrying weapons, and climbed over the wall. They tied up the owner, Xue Shugeng, and forced him to hand over silver dollars. It took them about an hour before they left with the loot towards the northwest. After the incident, it was found that the loss was about 800 yuan. Also, the home of Fan Quan, a resident near Fanxing Bridge outside the Great North Gate, was robbed at about 12:00 AM on the night of the 13th. All the dowry and miscellaneous items prepared for his daughter's marriage, as well as the money earned from selling rice, were robbed, with a loss of about 300 to 400 yuan. Both families reported the robbery to the county government and the district court to arrest the bandits. Zhou Daonan, the patrol officer of the first branch of the local Public Security Bureau, convened a winter defense meeting on the 15th to prevent future incidents.

Nantong 85

Third District of Water Police Meeting

The captains of the major brigades and police ships of the third district of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police were convened by the district chief, Zhu Aizhou, to meet on the 15th to discuss coastal defense along the Yangtze River. At the same time, the graduation ceremony of the full district officer and police cadre training class was held, and the newly formed Yangtze River Special Service Team was inspected.

Jiangyin 86

County Government Meeting on Public Security

The county government convened an emergency meeting on the afternoon of the 14th regarding the Xi'an Incident. Leaders of various agencies and organizations, as well as people from all walks of life, were in attendance to discuss public security matters in the county. After thorough deliberation, a public notice was jointly issued by the fortress commander and the county government. At the same time, telegrams were sent to the central government expressing support. Separately, various people's organizations and local residences jointly telegraphed Zhang Xueliang.

Xiong Zhu Gao Should Be Reprimanded

Former Director of Education Xiong Zhugao, in January of this year, arbitrarily moved the bureau's location, ordering elementary school students Fu Yancheng and Han Liang to transport public and private belongings. Parents of the students, Zhu Xinshan and others, filed a complaint with the Jiangsu Commissioner of Supervision. Zhu Chunli was appointed to investigate and submit an impeachment. After review by the Supervisory Yuan, it was deemed that disciplinary action should be taken. The Jiangsu Provincial Local Civil Service Disciplinary Committee decided that Xiong Zhugao should be reprimanded.

Yangzhou 87

Extortion Letter Demands Six Hundred Yuan

Ya Jianzhi, who opened the Yadecheng Oil Mill next to the Jingsi Temple in Dalu Township, Jiangdu County, prospered in business and was coveted by bandits. He recently received an extortion letter, roughly stating that by the end of the tenth lunar month, six hundred silver dollars wrapped in a white towel with a red flower on top should be sent to the Jingsi Temple public cemetery, and someone would come to collect it. Otherwise, vicious and cruel measures would be taken. The 14th was already the first day of the eleventh lunar month. Jing has not reported to the authorities nor complied with the demands, stating that he is quietly awaiting developments and likely has sufficient preventive measures in place.

Ningbo 88

Thirteen Refugees Rescued

Since the beginning of winter this year, pirates in the Zhejiang Sea have taken advantage of the situation and become rampant, with repeated cases of fishing boats being robbed. The Shipu Water Police received a report on the 12th that pirates were hiding fishermen refugees they had captured from the Northern Sea in Jiang'er Ao. They dispatched a team by boat to capture them that evening. When they arrived at Laolin Mountain, they encountered the pirate ship. Both sides immediately engaged in battle. As a result, the pirates were repelled. The team immediately rescued two large fishing cooperative boats and refugees, including Amu and thirteen others, in Jiang'er Ao. On the 13th, they were sent to the Shipu team headquarters and escorted by police to Shenjiamen.

Cixi 89

Protecting the East Township from a Major Fire

Ye A'lai, a farmer from the Yejia Jingfang in Cixi's East Township, hired a farmhand. On this day, he and his wife planned to go to the Chen family for a feast. They left a fire unattended while cooking, which ignited the accumulated firewood and caused a fire. At the same time, a gas lamp in a neighbor's house suddenly exploded during their celebration, igniting the floorboards. Fires broke out in both places simultaneously, causing widespread panic. Various volunteers rushed to the rescue upon hearing the alarm, but due to the drought and lack of water, and the fire spreading east and west, they were unable to extinguish it. It was not until after three o'clock that the fire was finally put out. It is estimated that more than seventy ordinary houses were destroyed, with losses exceeding forty thousand yuan.

Yuyao 90

Theater Performance in Yan Yan Township Leads to Trouble

Thugs in Yan Yan Township, southwest of Yuyao, hired a local opera troupe, which had been performing for several days. On the 12th, the county Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, dispatched District Chief Mou and police to the village to ban the performance. However, the thugs not only disobeyed but also incited more than three hundred able-bodied men and over a thousand people watching the performance to surround and disarm the police officers, and tie them up and beat them at the team's headquarters. Township Chief Shao Zongquan did not stop them, but falsely reported a robbery to the county. After the county Public Security Bureau sent a large contingent of police officers to the village, they rescued the injured police officer and took seven farmers involved in the incident to the county. Shao Ziying, the township chief's son, led more than twenty Baozhang to petition the county, claiming that the police officers were harassing the villagers. The county magistrate, considering Ziying as the instigator of the riot, ordered his detention and dismissed the Baozhang, sending them back to their villages. The Public Security Bureau also arrested Hu Zhihong, the fourth Baozhang, and brought him to the court for questioning.

Sports News

Our Country's Wrestling Master "Ape-Man" Huang Bochang Wrestles Down Miha. Miha is Incredibly Strong, Huang Repeatedly Suffers. In the Fifth Round, Miha is Lifted into the Air and Wrestled Down. 91

Our country's overseas Chinese wrestling master Huang Bochang wrestled with the famous Indian wrestler Miha last night at the St. George's Dance Hall. The audience was full, making it an unprecedentedly grand wrestling competition. The ferocity and tension of the fight were unseen before. Miha was as strong as an ox, while Huang was light and agile. In the fifth round, Huang used his quick skills to lift Miha into the air, quickly spun him three times, and wrestled him down, earning applause and cheers from the entire arena, deafeningly loud. In the sixth round, although Miha tried to retaliate, he was ultimately unsuccessful, and Huang won. The Chinese and foreign audience in the entire arena unanimously congratulated Huang repeatedly. A beautiful Western woman even went on stage to kiss Huang as a gesture of respect.

Wrestling is India's Specialty

Last night's program included four boxing matches and two wrestling matches. Another wrestling match was between an Indian, Habengsi, and Anderson, also in the heavyweight class. In less than five minutes, Anderson was wrestled down by Habengsi. Anderson could no longer fight and lost. It can be seen that wrestling is a specialty of the Indian people. After a ten-minute intermission, Huang Bochang and Miha took the stage.

Mr. Huang Wins by Skill

Miha weighs two hundred and twenty pounds, while Mr. Huang weighs two hundred and fifteen pounds. Both men have immense strength, like two tigers fighting. Even Tarzan the Ape-Man from novels would likely be no more than this. Miha relies entirely on strength, specializing in arm twists. Mr. Huang repeatedly suffered from this. Fortunately, Mr. Huang has many skills. After several struggles, he uses extremely fast methods to break free in unexpected ways. However, it is not easy for Mr. Huang to wrestle him down. However, several times he used a fierce blow to the forearm (cannot use boxing, only use the forearm to strike) and a flat kick with both feet (cannot kick with the toe), causing Miha unbearable pain.

No Winner in the First Four Rounds

The ferocity of the two men fighting was terrifying and breathtaking. Due to the difference in strength, Huang seemed to adopt a more defensive posture, making good use of skill. Every time it seemed hopeless, Mr. Huang was always able to break free and rise. The most interesting thing was that Mr. Huang used tickling to make his opponent release the hold, causing the entire arena to burst into laughter. The first four rounds were a draw, with no winner.

Huang Suddenly Performs a Stunning Masterpiece

In the fifth round, Mr. Huang launched a fierce attack as soon as he entered the arena. Miha was initially knocked down. Mr. Huang quickly rushed forward and butted him in the abdomen. In an instant, he lifted Miha above his head. The speed of his movement did not allow Miha to break free. Huang quickly turned in the middle of the stage, about half a minute, and forcefully wrestled Miha down, making him dazed and exhausted. Huang received applause and stomping from the audience, and the cheers were deafening. This method is the most difficult movement in wrestling and also the only way to win. To lift a man weighing two hundred and twenty pounds above his head and spin him three times before wrestling him down is truly difficult.

Miha's Retaliation Ultimately Fails

At the start of the sixth round, Miha tried to retaliate, repeatedly threatening Huang. He repeatedly twisted one of Huang's arms, or forcefully clamped Huang's head with both legs. Huang was finally able to break free and rise. This round ended without a winner. The match consisted of six rounds, each ten minutes long, with a one-minute break. As a result, Huang was judged the winner. The cheers from the entire arena were deafening. Countless people shook hands with Huang to congratulate him. A certain Western woman stepped forward to kiss him. Several Indian men jumped onto the stage, expressing their disagreement and challenging Huang. A Filipino then defended Huang and challenged the Indians. The referee announced that there would be another match next Saturday.

Last Night's West Youth Basketball. Jinan Overwhelms the Xin Team. 92

The first half was eighteen to twelve, resulting in forty-four to thirty. In the ordinary group, Zhongyi beat Shuizhuan by fifty-one to thirty-three.

Last night in the West Youth Basketball, Zhongyi beat Shuizhuan by fifty-one to thirty-three in the ordinary group, with the first half being twenty-seven to sixteen, an overwhelming lead. Yin Guiren and Wang Nanzhen penetrated three times again, scoring and returning, making it twenty-eight to twenty. The score became disparate. The Xin team quickly adjusted Ling Xianyang to the stage to replace Qu Xilin, showing some turning point. However, Feng Nianhua's one free throw and one miss only narrowed the gap to twenty-five to thirty, with no improvement. Jinan's Yin and Han then added three goals again. Cai Yanxiong added another free throw, and the score reached thirty-seven to twenty-five. The Xin team was largely doomed from here on out. Not long after, Cai Yanxiong was sent off for four fouls. Yan Lian entered as a substitute. Han Zhenyuan scored again. The Xin team was already fourteen points behind. At this time, Qu Xilin was transferred to replace Sun Baoqing, and the connection became active again. However, Jinan was now focusing on defense, making it difficult to break through. Lu Zhongen and Ling Xianyang only relied on long shots, each scoring two goals, but Jinan's Yong attacked under the basket twice again, and Yin Guiren added a penalty, so the Xin team gained more than it lost, with forty-four to twenty-nine still fifteen points apart, before long Lu Zhongen had a free shot due to Han Zhenyuan's foul, and the silver whistle sounded at this time, Jinan beat the Xin team at forty-four to thirty.

Tian Bo Lie Returns to England by Steamer and Publishes a Letter to Chinese Historians (Part 2) 103

In this era of specialization, this is indeed the path of proper development. Allow me to list several such international organizations and briefly describe their operations. First, there are several international scientific organizations, such as the "Union Académique Internationale" (International Union of Academies). This union is particularly useful in language-related matters and has helped to ease national jealousies. One of its organs is of particular interest to me and especially relevant to Chinese historians, namely the "International Committee of Historical Sciences". Japan is a member of this committee and is now preparing to take full advantage of its position. I am very pleased that she is a member. All countries in this committee are friendly to each other, and I hope that China will soon appear in this committee as well. China is not yet a member, and has never been one, but I hope she will become a member soon, so that in the 1936 International Congress of Historical Sciences, there will not be only one country presenting its views on the history of the Far East. On the other hand, it can certainly show that representatives of various countries can express their different views and knowledge. The Committee on Intellectual Cooperation emerged after the Great War, and all its activities began in this era. I have great faith in this committee, but I would also like to state that institutions that emerged after the war are easier to carry out than those that emerged before the war. The achievements of the International Committee of Historical Sciences are even better, because it is a pre-war institution. After the war, it not only existed, but also became the first of all pre-war international organizations to unite the former warring countries on terms of equality and friendship. They had already achieved this by 1926, while the "Union Académique Internationale" only managed to do so nine years later, in 1935. Therefore, we help to resolve national and racial jealousies. In various international cooperative undertakings, we feel that we can work together with all the countries that join. We already have forty-two countries that have joined, including Soviet Russia. China and its historians have never cooperated with us. Today, I am reading the best quarterly bibliography of English books on China, which only requires careful sorting and selection by historians to be suitable for the "International Bibliography of Historical Sciences". This publication was published from 1926 to 1934, and the 1935 issue is being prepared. Chinese historians have not yet sponsored this kind of compilation work, and the same is true for other cooperative undertakings. The journal of the International Committee of Historical Sciences publishes reports from many countries, mostly on the history of journalism and publishing, the history of calligraphy, and the historical teaching of schools and universities, as well as historical charts. China has opportunities to speak on these matters, but nothing has been heard from Chinese historians and their historical activities. This is your failure, not the fault of ignorant Western historians. We want to understand you, we give you the opportunity to publish, but we cannot find you. This is truly what is called "hungry sheep looking upwards, but not being fed". Please tell us about your historical activities, not as propagandists and politicians do, but as scholars and scientific historians do. This request is certainly not excessive. The above only describes what Chinese historians living in your country can do, as well as contributions that can be practically completed within China. In addition, there is one more thing that China can contribute: in 1938, she should send one or two famous historical scholars as representatives to Zurich, Switzerland, to participate in the discussion of Far Eastern history. I hope that both China and Japan will have representatives in this meeting. As far as I have inquired, the foundation of Chinese historical scholarship is so solid that if it is supported by its representative historical scholars, the request to join as a member state will definitely be successful. Admission requires the approval of a general meeting of more than forty countries, but if China comes knocking on the door, I don't think we will let them wait long. Chinese historians, this is your best opportunity to show yourselves! When the new country requests to join the meeting in Zurich, Switzerland, I will still be the president. If I can preside over the admission of the oldest nation in the world today—China—into our assembly of forty nations, it would be one of the most honorable moments of my life! (End)

Committee for the Preparation of the China Normal Education Society Designated 105

Several dozens of people, including Ministry of Education secretaries, counselors, directors, section chiefs, specialists, supervisors, compilers, and staff members, as well as personnel from academic organizations and educational institutions in Beijing, initiated the organization of the China Normal Education Society (formerly named the China Normal Education Association, now named the China Normal Education Society). It has been reported in previous issues of the society's journal that various places outside Beijing, such as Liu Jihong, President of Henan University, Huang Baofu, President of Qixia Rural Normal School, Gao Jiansi, President of Jiangsu Education College, Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai Hujiang University, Tai Shulong, Dean of the Education College of Shanghai Great China University, and Zheng Tonghe, President of Shanghai Middle School, have joined the initiators. In Beijing, more than ten people, including Legislative Yuan member Zhao Shuting, Central University professors Ai Xianzhou, Zhang Shiyi, Chang Daozhi, Central Political Professor Wang Diancun, and well-known figures in the education sector such as Lu Buqing, have also joined the initiators. It is heard that the society already has more than eighty initiators. Within days, in accordance with the procedures for organizing social groups, the reasons for the initiation and the list of initiators will be sent to the Party headquarters for record. After the initiators' meeting, Ministry of Education Senior Secretary Ma Zongrong, Directors Lei Zhen and Gu Shusen, Counselor Chen Shizhen, Legislative Yuan member Zhao Naichuan, Wu Yifang, President of Jinling Women's College of Arts and Sciences, Ai Wei, Dean of the Education College of Central University, Wang Maozu, Director of the Education Department of the Central Political School, Zheng Tonghe of Shanghai Middle School, Liu Zhanen of Hujiang University, and He Shuangqiu of Great China University will be nominated as a preparatory committee of eleven people to organize a preparatory meeting to prepare for the establishment. After the society is established, it will conduct research on normal education academics, introduce teaching methods, and produce films on normal teaching methods to facilitate the observation and imitation of teachers across the country, which will be of great help in promoting compulsory education and social education.

Doctor of Jurisprudence He Haiyan Will Return to China 107

Mr. He Haiyan graduated from the Faculty of Arts of Shanghai Datong University and the Faculty of Law of Soochow University. His thesis was highly praised by the legal community and he was awarded a Doctor of Jurisprudence degree. He passed through Japan and went to investigate the current situation of the country's judiciary, and also conducted in-depth research with professors at Tokyo Imperial University, especially gaining insights into commercial law. He has taken a ship to return to China and is expected to arrive in Shanghai in one or two days.

The American rate against the French rate rose by 0.375. The Central Bank's posted rates revealed that both England and the United States were unchanged. The Customs Gold Unit fell by 0.02. The exchange rate market opened in the morning with a selling price for near-term English exchange at 1 shilling 2.4375 pence and American exchange at $29.50. Compared to the previous close, the English rate loosened by 0.0625 and the American rate loosened by 0.125. After the opening, a certain bank offered near-term rates, and foreign banks pushed to buy near-term rates and offered forward rates, immediately leading to loosening. The situation was still optimistic. HSBC's posted rates revealed that both England and the United States were unchanged. Although it was hardening, it was still in flux. Afterwards, Japanese banks forcefully dumped Eastern exchange. The Bank of Communications and the Central Bank regulated American dollars. The silver equalization tax was revealed to have risen by one cent, but it still loosened because banks were dumping. In the afternoon, due to rumors unfavorable to the current situation, and sentiment turned good again, Chinese merchants repeatedly bought back, gradually tightening again. The Bank of Communications continued to trade foreign exchange with foreign banks to harmonize the situation. The Indian silver initially fell slightly by one anna, and then rebounded by one anna, without much impact. The closing selling price for near-term English exchange was 1 shilling 2.40625 pence and American dollars at $29.4375. Compared to the previous close, the English rate loosened by 0.03125 and hardened by 0.0625. The forward rates loosened by 0.0625 for English exchange and hardened by 0.125 for American dollars. Textiles Cloth Prices Deviate from Actual Sales; Although Sales are Dull, the Market Shows an Increase 119

Yesterday's cotton cloth market was sluggish, and the situation was very chaotic. People were waiting to see how the Xi'an Incident would develop. Demand in various places was weak. Orders were being delivered as usual, keeping people busy, but new transactions were rare. The morning yarn and cotton market was stable. Cloth prices remained high despite weak actual sales. Colleagues distributed plain coarse cloth, fine cloth, fine twill, and coarse twill from various Chinese and foreign factories. Spot goods were sold slightly. The market for coarse cloth and coarse twill remained unchanged. Fine cloth, fine twill, and heavy cloth fell by 0.05. Total transactions were over 200 pieces. Printed direct tribute, serge, colored tribute, and satin sold at a flat price. Spot sales were not smooth. Printing and dyeing factories were very idle. Near noon, yarn prices suddenly rebounded by $4. Bullish sentiment spread throughout the market. In the afternoon, the yarn market continued to rise, stimulating the cloth market. Selling prices suddenly increased by 0.1 to 0.15. This created a deviation from the current sluggish sales. Actual sales were not initially stimulated, but the market prices rose by 0.15, it is said.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms' Silk Purchases Gradually Nearing Agreement 123

White Filature Silk Slightly Sold Yesterday

The silk market has felt rather sluggish lately. Yesterday, the New York exchange market showed a stable surge. Various grades of silk, both nearby and from distant locations in Japan, the United States, and France, experienced slight increases or maintained their original prices. However, the prices for Japanese silk in New York and other areas showed some softening. It is estimated that daily Chinese and Guangdong silk prices were down by three to five cents compared to last Saturday. However, silk purchases by foreign firms are gradually nearing agreement. Consequently, white filature silk in Shanghai has seen slightly increased sales. Current market prices cannot be compared to the previous high prices. Recently, ordinary B-grade 20-22 denier silk, without evenness, sold for 710 yuan, which is considered relatively average. Sales of Indian firm silk gradually met demand yesterday, so transactions gradually decreased. There is still no improvement in silk for domestic use.

Local News

Mayor Wu Replied to Acting President Kong Yesterday Stating He Would Lead Shanghai Citizens to Support Central Policies 124

Since Zhang Xueliang's mutiny and kidnapping of the Commander-in-Chief in Xi'an, Kong Xiangxi, the Vice President of the Executive Yuan, has been acting as the head of the Executive Yuan. On the 13th, he sent a telegram to the authorities of various provinces and cities, expressing his willingness to work together and strive to ensure national security in accordance with the established policies of President Chiang. Upon receiving the telegram, Mayor Wu Tiecheng of this city sent a reply to Acting President Kong yesterday, stating: "Respected Acting President Kong of the Executive Yuan in Nanjing, I have respectfully received your telegram. The news of the Xi'an Incident has caused immense distress and indignation. President Chiang has struggled arduously for many years with unwavering loyalty to the country. The lives of the people depend on him. National unity has already taken shape. We, who support the leader and work together for national salvation, are still afraid of falling short. Yet, a sudden change has occurred within our ranks, a most extraordinary event. The foundation of the nation is shaken, and our hearts are filled with grief. Wu Tiecheng is unworthy, but I will lead the citizens of Shanghai to unanimously support the policies of the Central Government in order to fulfill the expectations and local responsibilities. Maintaining order and stabilizing the people's hearts are the most urgent tasks. Currently, government affairs are proceeding as usual, and the local area is peaceful. Please ease your concerns and provide instructions so that we may follow them. I am filled with anticipation. Respectfully, Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai. [Seal]"

Jing-Gan Railway Loan, Initial Disbursement of One Million Yuan 125

Zhou Zuomin has Returned to Shanghai

In order to expand the Xuancheng-Guixi Railway, the Ministry of Railways used 14 million yuan of Jing-Gan Railway construction bonds as collateral to borrow from eight banks and savings societies, including Bank of Communications, China Farmers Bank, Jincheng Bank, Dalu Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Salt Industry Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Society. After the contract was agreed upon, it was signed by the banks on the evening of the 11th. Zhou Zuomin, the General Manager of Jincheng Bank and representative of the banking group, took the signed contract to Nanjing to be signed by Zhang Gongquan, the Minister of Railways. It has now been signed and Zhou returned to Shanghai yesterday, distributing the contract to the lending banks for safekeeping and verification. The lending banks will first pay 3 million yuan proportionally, which will be collected by Jincheng Bank and remitted to the Ministry of Railways. The remaining funds will be disbursed according to the contract in January, April, July, and September of next year.

Shanghai-Shaanxi Telegrams Restored Last Night 126

According to information from the local transportation authorities, the telegraph lines between Shanghai and Xi'an were interrupted after the Shaanxi Incident occurred. However, they were completely repaired and resumed communication at approximately 8:00 PM yesterday. Due to the heavy volume of telegrams, there may be slight delays in commercial telegrams.

Mail Service as Usual, Parcel Service Temporarily Suspended

The Shanghai Postal Administration announced yesterday that mail to Xi'an, Weinan, Xianyang, and other locations in Shaanxi Province, including express mail, registered mail, and airmail, will be delivered as usual. If communication to these locations is interrupted, the post office will make every effort to ensure delivery as quickly as possible. However, parcel service to Weinan, Xi'an, and other locations beyond Tongguan has been temporarily suspended as of yesterday to avoid errors.

Eurasia Airline Parcel Route Temporarily Suspended

The Eurasia Aviation Company's Shanghai-Xinjiang route is scheduled to fly west on Tuesdays and Fridays and east on Wednesdays and Saturdays. Today, the east-bound flight will proceed to Shanghai as scheduled, but the flight will not land at the Xi'an and Lanzhou stations for the time being. As for the Lanzhou-Baotou parcel route, which is scheduled to fly north on Wednesdays and Saturdays and south on Tuesdays and Fridays, and includes the Lanzhou, Ningxia, and Baotou stations, flights will be temporarily suspended to ensure passenger safety.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Advocates Donating New Year Savings to Support Suiyuan 127

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has issued a notice advocating for saving all expenses during the New Year and donating the savings to support Suiyuan. The notice states: "This time, the bandit-puppets have invaded Suiyuan. Our brave and loyal soldiers at the front line are fighting bloody battles in the freezing weather. Bailin Temple and Xila Mulun Temple have been successively recovered. Now, they are advancing towards Shangdu, and the good news is spreading rapidly, shaking the nation. Shanghai, being in the rear, should save unnecessary expenses as much as possible and donate generously to encourage the morale of the soldiers in this prelude to the revival of the nation. The New Year is approaching, and there is a custom of exchanging New Year gifts and sending greeting cards, which amounts to a considerable expense nationwide. At this critical time for the nation, when we are preoccupied with resisting the enemy, this annual extravagance is precisely when our people should be diligent and endure hardships, share life and death with the soldiers at the front line, and focus on relieving anxieties rather than celebrating. If we can use this unnecessary expenditure for the soldiers fighting the enemy, and if all the people share this sentiment, a substantial amount of money can be raised. The Chamber has taken up the advocacy of the insurance industry association, believing that it is essential. Therefore, we are announcing this in the newspapers, hoping that our compatriots across the country will uphold this proposition and actively promote it to achieve this great undertaking. If you agree, please deposit your savings with the banks and money shops designated by the Suiyuan Bandit Suppression Comfort and Rescue Committee, which is jointly formed by our chamber, etc. We anxiously await your contributions."

The Beijing-Jiangxi Railway Loan 145

First Payment of Three Million Yuan 146

To Be Used for the People Who Have Already Returned to Shanghai

In order to extend the Xuan Cheng to Gui Xi Railway, the Ministry of Railways used the 14 million yuan in construction bonds for the Beijing-Jiangxi Railway to fully borrow from eight banks and trust companies, including Bank of Communications, Chinese Farmers, Jincheng, Dalu, Zhongnan, Yanye, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Association. After the contract was agreed upon, the banks first signed it. On the evening of the 11th, the president of Jincheng Bank, Zhou Zuomin, the general representative of the banking group, carried it to Beijing and handed it over to the Minister of Railways, Gong Quan, for signature. It has already been signed and completed. Zhou brought it back to Shanghai on the previous day and distributed it to the borrowing banks for safekeeping. Each borrowing bank will pay 3 million yuan first as an example. Jincheng Bank will collect and deliver the payment, and the rest will be paid according to the contract in January, April, July, and September of next year.

Guangdong Bank Shanghai Branch Reopens Yesterday Morning, Receiving New Deposits of Ten Million Yuan 147

Central News Agency reports that the Guangdong Bank Shanghai Branch reopened on the morning of the 15th, with Chinese and British flags prominently displayed at the entrance. Several Chinese and Western police officers from the Public Works Department provided security. The bank's Chairman, T.V. Soong, Executive Directors Wu Tiecheng, Deng Mianren, Huo Baoshu, and others arrived around 9:00 AM to preside over the reopening, though no ceremony was held. Prominent figures from various sectors in Shanghai, both Chinese and foreign, including Xu Kan, Ye Gongchuo, Li Shizeng, Zhao Dihua, Chen Xing, Zhou Zuomin, Zhang Peishen, Chen Guangfu, Feng Gengguang, Zhang Tingfu, Lin Kanghou, Bei Songsun, Xi Demao, Shen Shuyu, Zhu Runsheng, and others, visited to offer their congratulations. They were received by General Manager Zhang Rongpu and all the bank's staff, and refreshments were served on the fifth floor. Half of the bank's existing deposits were converted into shares, and the other half was issued as unsecured bonds, all of which have been distributed. New deposits received in the morning exceeded five million yuan, and the total for the afternoon is expected to reach ten million yuan. It is also reported that the bank has joined the Shanghai Bankers Association and is in negotiations to restore its membership, which is not expected to be a problem. As for the clearing house, the bank was originally the 23rd clearing bank. Since its closure, no other bank has replaced it. Due to the late notification, it was unable to resume immediately, and will temporarily entrust the Bank of Communications, Shanghai, and other banks to handle its clearing. It is expected that the procedures will be completed by the end of the month, and clearing will be resumed.

The Guangdong Bank Shanghai Branch opened yesterday morning. The bank's Chairman, T.V. Soong, issued a statement saying that the Guangdong Bank was the first commercial bank established in South China, with branches throughout overseas. Among the banks in South China, it has been the leading bank for many years. Unfortunately, due to the global economic downturn and the bank's improper response, it was affected and temporarily suspended operations. However, due to its strong foundation and excellent reputation, the domestic and foreign creditors supported a thorough reorganization shortly after the suspension. As a result, the bank's financial situation recovered, and a large amount of new capital was quickly raised. Many new businesses in China were founded by people from Guangdong, but the progress of these businesses requires sound financial institutions as their backing to be successful. People from Guangdong everywhere are eager for the bank to reopen soon. The Shanghai financial community also has unlimited hopes for the future development of the Guangdong economy and especially hopes that the bank will be restored in time so that there will be a bank representing the merchants and people of Guangdong to jointly develop. The Hong Kong head office and the Guangzhou branch reopened on the 23rd and 25th of last month, respectively, and have received enthusiastic support from the government and the public. The atmosphere is excellent. The Shanghai and Hankou branches opened today, and overseas branches will also reopen in the shortest possible time. Shanghai is the center of industry and commerce in the country and the hub of finance. The business tasks of the Shanghai branch, assisting the businesses of the people of Guangdong, and mediating various commercial interests, should be given special attention to fulfill the bank's special mission. Chairman T.V. Soong told a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency yesterday that after Guangdong Bank prepared for reopening according to the negotiated plan, the Hong Kong branch first reopened on the 23rd of last month, the Guangzhou branch also reopened on the 25th of last month, and the Shanghai and Hankou branches reopened at the same time today. The overseas San Francisco and Taishan branches will also reopen on a regular basis. As for the staff of each branch, they are all people with banking experience. He also provided a copy of the negotiated plan, which is recorded as follows: Hong Kong Guangdong Bank Limited Negotiated Plan: (1) Apply to the Hong Kong High Court to revoke the liquidation of Guangdong Bank Limited (hereinafter referred to as the Bank). This report was submitted by the Bank's directors on September 4, 1935. (2) The Bank's capital of 8,665,600 yuan (divided into 216,640 shares, each with a face value of 40 yuan, fully paid up, referred to as ordinary shares in this plan) will be reduced to 1,083,200 yuan, divided into 116,640 shares, each with a face value of 5 yuan. This method of reducing share capital is to deduct the amount of losses or assets that cannot be represented from the fully paid-up share capital, that is, to reduce the previous 216,640 shares by 35 yuan per share, and to reduce the nominal value of all the Bank's ordinary shares from 40 yuan to 5 yuan per share. (3) Authorize the Bank to issue the following types of shares to increase the Bank's capital: (A) 200,000 shares with a fully paid-up value of 10 yuan per share. This type of share is called the first preferred share and has the right to a fixed cumulative preferred dividend, calculated at an annual interest rate of 8% on the fully paid-up share capital. It is paid first from the annual profits, and its share capital rank is higher than all other types of shares. (B) Second preferred shares of 10 yuan per share, which are subscribed by the Bank's unsecured creditors. In the future, the Bank will provide shares of equal value to each creditor at half the value of their debt. Creditors who accept this type of share should regard it as compensation for half of their debt. This type of share has a fixed cumulative preferred dividend right calculated at an annual interest rate of 4%, which is paid from the profits after the first preferred shares, and its distribution of dividends is after the above-mentioned first preferred shares with an 8% interest rate and before the ordinary shares. (C) Holders of the first and second preferred shares have one vote per share held and are subject to Articles 113 to 125 of the Bank's articles of association regarding shareholders' voting rights. Holders of the Bank's ordinary shares have one vote for every two shares held. The provisions of Articles 113 to 125 of the Bank's articles of association must be applied separately. (4) In any year, if the company's profits at the end of the year, after deducting enough to distribute, (A) the above-mentioned first preferred share dividend, (B) the second preferred share dividend, if there is still a surplus, it will be divided equally between the holders of the first preferred shares and the holders of ordinary shares. The method of distribution is that if the dividend on ordinary shares does not exceed 4% of the value of each hundred, it will be distributed according to the dividend on ordinary shares. However, in any case, the equal amount of distribution shall not exceed the fixed amount. (5) The amount of the second preferred shares that the Bank's unsecured creditors should receive shall not exceed half of the amount of debt owed by the Bank to them. No such shares shall be given for odd numbers less than ten yuan. (6) The Bank will issue bearer bonds to each unsecured creditor to offset half of the remaining debt owed by the Bank. This amount will still be counted as the amount owed by the Bank, but no interest will be calculated. It will be amortized and repaid to each creditor, or their executor, or administrator of the estate, or assignee in five years (so that each bond can be redeemed in full). Each installment shall not be less than one-fifth of the said half. The first installment shall be paid within twelve months after this plan becomes binding. This bond may be used by the holder at any time to offset the debt owed by the holder to the Bank before the Bank's suspension of operations, or to purchase or exchange any of the Bank's assets. (7) When a meeting of creditors is held in accordance with the order of the court, five supervisors and one special manager should be elected immediately to handle all the affairs required for the implementation of this plan, including the review of debt amounts and the management of the Bank's usual business, all of which are included from the date this plan becomes binding until the election of new directors. (8) Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in this plan, if any of the Bank's creditors have the right to full compensation prior to other debts based on Article 251 of the Companies Ordinance of 1932 or other provisions, the Supervisory Committee shall, within four weeks after this plan becomes binding, allocate funds from the Bank's assets to fully compensate them. (9) After this plan is approved, the directors should immediately resign from their positions. Before the new directors are elected in accordance with Article 10 of this plan, the supervisors and special managers, in accordance with the provisions of this plan, should manage the business on behalf of them, in addition to complying with the various provisions of this plan, and be responsible for clearing all the benefits received to the new directors. Any debts incurred due to public service and various expenses incurred in the implementation of this plan shall be compensated by the Bank in full. (10) The Supervisory Committee or the Board of Directors has the right to pay in cash the amount of mortgage debt that has not been recovered, such as odd numbers less than twenty yuan or ten yuan. (11) The term "unsecured creditor" in this plan should be interpreted to include all creditors whose debts have been recognized by the Supervisory Committee (excluding secured creditors and creditors mentioned in Article 8). (12) Within four months after this plan becomes binding, a shareholders' meeting of various types of shareholders must be convened to elect the Bank's directors in accordance with the provisions of the articles of association. (13) Once the unsecured creditors of this Bank accept the various provisions in this plan that are beneficial to the creditor, their various claims against this Bank and its assets should be regarded as having been fully settled. (14) Within twelve weeks after this plan becomes binding, at least 30,000 preferred shares must be collected and the share capital must be fully paid up. Otherwise, the Supervisory Committee may, with the approval of the court, declare that this plan has failed. Once such a declaration is made, liquidation procedures must be carried out, and the various provisions of this plan will be invalid. (15) If it is necessary to amend the memorandum of association and the articles of association due to the implementation of this plan, they must be amended accordingly. (16) All public fees and miscellaneous fees required for this plan and the implementation of the plan should be paid by this Bank. (17) The court should approve any modifications or conditions that the court deems appropriate to this plan. (18) Except as otherwise provided in the above, the various provisions of this plan shall not prejudice any pledge, lien, or mortgage.

Situation of Comforting the Troops

Luo Youxuan, the representative of the Shanghai Committee for Comforting and Rescuing the Suiyuan Bandit Suppression Army in Suiyuan, recently returned to Shanghai from Xi'an and reported on the situation of comforting the troops in Suiyuan, saying that when the Shanghai Comfort Group arrived in Suiyuan, Youxuan was entrusted by Mr. Wang, Lin, and Huang to temporarily stay in Suiyuan, partly to comfort the soldiers at the front line and partly to make on-the-spot investigations. The process is reported as follows: On November 25 and 26, a general inspection was made in Suiyuan Province, and the Suiyuan Woolen Mill was visited. The factory is very small, powered by electricity, and has about 150 employees. The products are felt, tweed, etc. The quality is good. Except for the dyes, the rest are domestic raw materials. Ordinary people have a fairly adequate life because of the sparse population and the relatively fertile land. The wages of hired farmers are about 40 to 50 yuan per year. The entire Suiyuan can offset income and expenditure in terms of economics and finance (the total expenditure of the provincial government is only more than 80,000 yuan). Therefore, although the population is only more than 2 million, it is still enough to maintain the local area and be the vanguard of resisting foreign insults. Now the order in Suiyuan is quite good, there are no beggars in the provincial city, and there are not many unemployed. On November 27, he set off from Suiyuan, passed through Wuchuan, and went to Bailingmiao, the foremost of our army (the temple is 360 li from Suiyuan Province, but actually 500 li). Along the way, there are 120 li of uninhabited grasslands. It has snowed now, and the temperature is about minus 20 to 25 degrees Celsius. It is extremely difficult for our army to operate. He arrived at the temple at 10:30 that night. The temple is surrounded by mountains, like a city wall. There is a small plain in the middle, and a stream of water surrounds it in the back. The temple is built between the plain and the stream, with more than 200 houses. The main hall is beautifully constructed. In the life of thousands of miles of grasslands, only tents are holy relics. The temple is a holy place for Mongolians in terms of religion, and a channel for Outer Mongolia and Xinjiang in terms of transportation. The Japanese have been operating in this place for four years. According to personal superficial estimates, the operation of the Bailingmiao special agency is at least more than 5 million yuan. This time, the puppet Mongolian army was defeated, and the items left by the Japanese, the number of which can be counted, are more than 20,000 bags of flour, 500,000 jin of coal, 300-400 boxes of gasoline, and 30-40 new-style stoves. The head of the special agency, Shengdao Jiaofang, and more than 20 assistant personnel are stationed in the temple all year round. However, according to Sui espionage, the Japanese have spent 40 million yuan in special funds for the special agencies commanded by the Guandong Army in Duolun, Jiabusi, Bailingmiao, Heishatu, Dingyuanying, and Ejina. Previously, there were regular air flights to the above-mentioned places, and the special personnel in Bailingmiao all studied the Chinese language and studied Chinese affairs. After careful investigation, no books studying the Soviet Union were found, and no one was learning Russian. Now the defense of our side of the temple is consolidated, and the morale is particularly strong. It is a pity that it is too far away from Suiyuan. In the event of a major war, it will be difficult to respond. However, the operation of the factory is also similarly difficult. On the 28th, he returned to Suiyuan, and on the 30th, he arrived at Pingdiquan. At the right time, the 13th Army of Tang arrived at the place and was preparing to advance the construction and enrich the defense line. Solid fortifications have been built in Fengzhen, Datong, and the Taihang Mountains. Strongholds have been established in key areas of Jin and Sui, and an offensive defense has been adopted. Although Taiyuan does not advocate immediately taking Shangdu and Zhangbei, it is preparing to deal with the war. The expression of unity from top to bottom in Jin and Sui is very obvious, and the central government and the local government are quite consistent. Political preparation is also gradually becoming more comprehensive. He left B on the 5th of this month, arrived in Xi'an on the 8th, and left Xi'an on the evening of the 10th to return to Shanghai.

Proposed Important Cases

The Shanghai General Labor Union's motion to the conference stated that, according to reports, Zhang Xueliang's troops suddenly rebelled in Xi'an and kidnapped the commander. The news was shocking. The association convened an emergency executive committee meeting this morning to discuss countermeasures. It was agreed that at this emergency time, the actions of all groups should be consistent and united to align their steps and respond to the situation. It was resolved to form a joint office of various groups, etc., and the record was recorded. In addition to sending letters to the outside world, the case was specially recorded and presented, and three members, Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, and Shao Xubai, were recommended to contact the former. After Zhu Xuefan supplemented the reasons for the proposal on the spot, the members discussed it, and they all believed that at the time of this incident, it was absolutely necessary to align their steps and express public opinion to comfort Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. It was proposed that representatives be sent to Xi'an when necessary. After discussion, it was decided to hand it over to the board of directors for deliberation and handling.

The details are recorded separately as follows:

Representatives Present

Those who attended yesterday included Wang Rutang, Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Li Dachao, Pan Gongzhan, Guan Jiongzhi, Qu Wenliu, Tai Shuangqiu, Zhao Jinqing, Wang Yiting, Chen Tiesheng, Wang Zhenchang, Wu Kaisheng, Zhu Shaoping, Lou Zhaonian, Le Zhenbao, Huang Ruisheng, Fan Shouyuan, Lu Bohong, Chen Qifen, Huang Renzhi, Wang Sifang, Chen Guangfu, Lu Yingen, Lu Xianglin, Yang Hansan, and more than 40 representatives from Daxia Automobile Company, Xintong Automobile Company, and Deda Automobile Company. Chairman's Report

General Fu Zuoyi led his subordinates to defend the border for the sake of national survival. Fortunately, the soldiers used their lives and were united. In the Battle of Bailingmiao, the enemy was defeated and fled. Looking forward to the future, we are very fortunate. However, when swords meet and bullets collide, our army's casualties are unavoidable. In addition, the snowy and icy weather and the dangerous transportation make it difficult and time-consuming to transport the wounded comrades in arms on the front line. Therefore, it is an urgent matter to rescue them. The association has always been committed to serving the society and dares not lag behind in national salvation work. Therefore, we have launched a fundraising campaign for ambulances to collect several cars and send them to the Red Cross for the exclusive use of rescuing wounded soldiers on the front line. This matter is of great importance and relies on the collective efforts of the people. In addition to raising donations from all parties to prepare for the purchase, we also request major automobile companies in the city to make special arrangements for the sale price and reduce the price in order to rescue the wounded soldiers for humanitarian reasons.

Car Purchase Method

The following car purchase methods are proposed: (1) These cars are specially negotiated for purchase from various companies, and a special discount is given according to the list price. (2) If a company agrees to sell a certain number of cars, the association will list the brand, list price, current sale price, and special discount separately in the donation advertisement to be a model. (3) The aforementioned vehicles will be sent to the Chinese Red Cross Society for the purpose of rescuing wounded soldiers on the front line and shall not be used for other purposes. (4) The purchase of vehicles will be jointly raised and collected by the association and various charitable organizations in the city. The donations will be deposited in the designated bank at any time and used for car purchase.

Organize Car Purchase Association

At that time, it was also decided to organize a car purchase committee, which will be formed by four representatives from the Charity Federation, the Chinese Red Cross Society, and the Road Association, namely Zhao Jinqing, Yan Fuqing, Qian Xinzhi, and Lou Zhaonian, and five representatives from the automobile companies, namely Smith, Myers, Frantmenkrow, and a representative from Youfu or Dachang to be determined, a total of nine people.

Launch of Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group: Tunam Dinner Party 152

Research on Nanyang Trade

The Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group, sponsored by the China Industrial Foreign Trade Association, has been working on the finalization of all matters since its return to the country. It is now known that the group's head and deputy heads, Gao Shiheng, Hu Shicheng, and Secretary Yang Zhonggao, are currently collecting materials and compiling reports separately. The content is extremely detailed and can serve as a guide for doing business in Nanyang. It will be finalized by the end of the year and printed, with publication expected in February next year. In addition, the group has launched the Tunam Dinner Party to study Nanyang trade and make long-term plans. The origin and rules of the association are listed below:

Origin

After the thorough observation and investigation of various parts of Nanyang by our inspection group, it is believed that it is indeed a good market, especially with great hope for the export of our country's goods. This is because our more than six million overseas Chinese, who control the authority of commercial economy, are all determined to promote and use domestic products. If we do not make good use of this great opportunity to promote the advancement of domestic goods to the south, wouldn't it be self-abandonment, failing the enthusiasm of overseas Chinese to protect the motherland? I, along with the inspection group colleagues, bear the heavy responsibility of expanding this overseas market for domestic goods. However, this matter is of great importance, and it is necessary to combine the spirit and intelligence of all our colleagues to conduct continuous research. By gathering ideas and benefiting from each other, we can receive twice the results with half the effort. However, we are all constrained by our duties, and it is not allowed by facts to gather and discuss at any time. Therefore, there is the launch of a dinner party, which is held once a month. It can not only maintain the feelings of the April group for a long time, but also use the conversations after tea and wine to exchange opinions and learn from each other, so that our country's goods can have a solid position in the Nanyang market in the future, and become brighter and larger. Therefore, the significance of this dinner party is not in the pursuit of food and drink, but in striving for the advancement of domestic goods to the south. Therefore, it is named Tunam. I believe that all colleagues will be happy to agree. This is the inspiration.

Rules

(1) All colleagues who participated in the Nanyang Commercial Inspection Group are eligible to be members. (2) The dinner party is scheduled for 7:00 PM on the 16th of each month. (3) The cost of each dinner is two yuan in legal tender per person, and those who are unable to attend for any reason must also pay. (4) Each time, one person on duty serves as the secretary, presiding over the seat arrangement, sending invitations, and collecting and paying funds. At each dinner, the next secretary is elected. (5) The association will last for a long time and will not be suspended midway. (6) Any domestic goods manufacturer who intends to develop trade in Nanyang and is willing to join the association as a member and conduct joint research may also participate with the introduction of two members.
