Zhang Qinghong Suddenly Reversed His Previous Testimony, Admitting That Bao and Yang Lived in His Home

Bao Gang's lawyer was sued by Cui Changgui, the bodyguard of Liu Huaizhi, the captain of the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, for inducing his fiancee Yang Yuehua to live in Zhang Qinghong's home in the third district of Chuansha. The local court filed a public prosecution, and Bao Gang and Bao's intermediary Zhang Xinkui were detained. Yesterday morning, Judge Xie of the local court opened the second criminal court for a continued trial and summoned Zhang Qinghong to court for further interrogation. However, Zhang Qinghong claimed that he graduated from Peidong Middle School and was not a classmate with Bao, and did not know Yang Yuehua and had never been to his home when he first appeared in court to testify. Before the special commissioner of the Jiangsu Supervisory Office, he also swore that if he did hide Yang Yuehua, he would accept the most severe punishment from the party. The latter's wife, Yu Shi, stated in court that Bao had lodged Yang Yuehua in her home in the name of a concubine, and had taken photos with Yang Yuehua, so the court repeatedly summoned Zhang Qinghong to court, but yesterday Zhang Qinghong's testimony reversed his previous testimony, claiming that he and Bao Gang were classmates at Chizhi University, Bao was in the law department, and he was in the political science department. My home is twelve miles away from Bao's home. On May 20 this year, he brought a woman and said it was a concubine. He first went to my district, and then he went to my home. The judge asked what your wife's surname was. He replied, "Xu", and also claimed that taking photos with Yang Yuehua and disguising himself as a man was done by my wife, Yao Shi. I don't know it was abducted, but I knew that Bao's family had a big wife, but I didn't know him. Yang Yuehua lived in my house for a total of two weeks, but I only saw her once because I was in the district. We are fellow villagers and classmates, so we took her in, and he also said that the wife and concubines did not get along, and living for two days is also a matter of human nature. After Bao Gang arrived in Chuansha on May 20, I have not seen him, but my wife said that he came twice in the middle. When Cui Changgui came to look for Yang Yuehua, my wife and I happened to come to Shanghai. At this point, the judge immediately said that you have sworn now, and telling lies will be punished for perjury. He replied, "Yes." At this point, Bao Gang was brought to court and asked how he would argue with Zhang Qinghong's testimony. Bao Yun said, "Absolutely not." At this point, he asked Zhang Xinkui, who claimed that he did not entice Yang Yuehua to the Dafang Hotel on May 12 to commit adultery with Bao Gang. At that time, I went back because my niece got married, and the township chief Lu Binglin can testify. The official often summons Lu Binglin to testify. He is forty-six years old, the head of Beicai Township in Nanhui, and a doctor. I only know about Zhang Xinkui's niece's wedding. I don't know how many days Zhang Xinkui lived at home. In short, his testimony is completely irresponsible. At this point, Cui Changgui and Yang Yuehua went to court and claimed that after the couple quarreled, Bao Gang took advantage of the opportunity to have illicit relations with Yang Yuehua three times at the Dafang Hotel, and then intimidated and abducted her to Zhang Qinghong's home for hiding, where I found her. County Magistrate Sprayed with Acid Case: Mid-Course Incident. Plaintiff Accuses Lawyer Gu Changyuan of Destroying Evidence and Using Perjury to Collude. Prosecutor Indicts After Investigation. 161

Xu Xueseng, the former magistrate of Zhangye County, Gansu Province, and head of the Opium Prohibition Bureau, a native of Songjiang, was splashed with nitric acid on his face in the French Concession's Wangzhi Road in March of this year. Gao Jinsheng, the perpetrator, was apprehended on the spot and sentenced to four years in prison by the Second Special District Court. The case is currently under appeal in the Supreme Court. Subsequently, Xu also filed a criminal self-indictment with the Shanghai District Court, accusing his fellow townsman, Zhu Guanghan, of instigating Chen Axi to instruct Gao Jinsheng to harm Xu, requesting punishment. The case was initially heard by Judge Wu Deying, but because Judge Wu was transferred to the Jiangsu High Court branch in Xuzhou, Judge Yu Lude took over the case. Unexpectedly, while Judge Yu was investigating, he was recently transferred to become an execution judge. Therefore, the case was transferred again to Judge Liu Bojun for a new hearing, scheduled to continue at 2:00 PM today. Details have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Unexpectedly, while the case was under detailed investigation and no decision had been made, an incident occurred. Since the case began, the defendant Zhu Guanghan hired lawyer Gu Changyuan to represent him in his defense. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff Xu Xueseng recently discovered that lawyer Gu had committed crimes such as destroying evidence and colluding with perjury in this case. Therefore, he filed a complaint with the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office. The Prosecutor's Office approved the complaint, and Prosecutor Wang Jiamei conducted a detailed investigation. The Prosecutor's Office believes that a public prosecution should be initiated, and the original indictment is transcribed below. Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office Indictment: Defendant Gu Changyuan, 46 years old, native of Jiaxing, is under the custody of lawyer Zou Shengshi. Fang Aliu, 27 years old, native of Ningbo, is in custody. The defendant is charged with evidence destruction and perjury in the Criminal Case No. 4554 of the 25th year of the Republic of China. The prosecutor has completed the investigation of the case and believes that a public prosecution should be initiated. The defendant's criminal facts, evidence, and the applicable legal provisions are listed below: (Criminal Facts) In May of this year, Xu Xueseng filed a self-indictment with the Criminal Division of this court, accusing Zhu Guanghan of instigating Gao Jinsheng to harm his body. Zhu Guanghan selected lawyer Gu Changyuan as his defense counsel. Gu Changyuan went to the Shanghai First Special District Court Detention Center on May 16th, May 23rd, and June 9th to meet with Gao Jinsheng, instigating him to conceal his testimony and promising him 100 yuan as a reward. Gao Jinsheng had asked his aunt through a letter from the detention center to request payment from Gu Changyuan. Fang Aliu, as Gao Jinsheng's sworn brother, was well aware of the situation and had previously testified under oath in the Criminal Division of this court. The letter from his aunt was obtained and presented to the court as evidence. However, during the court's investigation, Fang Aliu suddenly reversed his previous testimony in an attempt to exonerate Gu Changyuan, and he also testified under oath. (Evidence and Applicable Legal Provisions) Gu Changyuan went to the Shanghai Second Special District Court Detention Center to meet with Gao Jinsheng three times during Xu Xueseng's self-indictment in this court against Zhu Guanghan for instigating harm, as evidenced by the visitation log there. Gao Jinsheng sent a letter from the detention center to his aunt and uncle "Fang Aliu's aunt and uncle," which stated, "This afternoon, lawyer Gu visited me at the detention center. I told him all the details. Mr. Gu promised me 100 yuan. Now I'm asking Mr. Wu in his letter to quickly go to lawyer Gu's residence to collect the money." This letter was sent out by someone and was not inspected by the detention center. Although Gao Jinsheng did not admit to it, there was another letter issued by the detention center stating, "There is no need to see lawyer Gu now. They will come to see me later." The inspection stamp affixed to this letter has been verified by the Second Special District Prison, and it matches the prison's official stamp. The reply letter No. 462 dated October 29 of this year, both letters' handwriting, has also been identified as written by the same person. "Reference to the Identification Report." Gu Changyuan is Zhu Guanghan's defense counsel, and Gao Jinsheng did not entrust him with anything, so there was no need to meet with him. Even less reason to pay Gao Jinsheng 100 yuan as a reward. Now, during the meeting, he not only promised a reward, but also, based on Fang Aliu's testimony in the Criminal Division of this court on October 12 of this year, "Zhu Guanghan spent money to settle Gao Jinsheng's family after Gao Jinsheng harmed Xu Xueseng with acid," it is known that Gao Jinsheng's harm to Xu Xueseng was indeed instigated by Zhu Guanghan. Gu Changyuan, as Zhu Guanghan's defense counsel, naturally did not want Gao Jinsheng to testify in court and conceal the truth. As a result of the reward and collusion, Gao Jinsheng was willing to take the blame alone and never attacked Zhu Guanghan. Gu Changyuan's crime of instigating the concealment of testimony is indeed credible. According to Article 29, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, he should be considered an instigator of Article 165 of the same law. Fang Aliu had previously testified in the Criminal Division of this court that he had been friends with Gao Jinsheng for six years, that the letter issued by Gao Jinsheng in the detention center was obtained from his aunt's house, and that the letter with the inspection stamp was also said to be written by Gao Jinsheng. His testimony was detailed and he swore an oath. Now, on November 25, regarding the case of Gu Changyuan instigating concealment of testimony, his testimony is inconsistent with Gao Jinsheng and completely denies his previous testimony, which is obviously perjury. He has committed the crime of Article 168 of the Criminal Law. It is appropriate to file a prosecution in accordance with Article 230, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law. Please try the case according to law. Respectfully submitted to the Criminal Division of this court. December 7, 25th year of the Republic of China. Prosecutor Wang Jiamei.

Residents of Lixing Town Petition for Changes to River Dredging Plan 164

Regarding the East and West Zhu Family Gully Issue

The dredging of the East and West Zhu Family Gully in the Lixing District of Pudong requires passing through Dutai River, which will obstruct the houses of the town's households. Therefore, the residents of the town petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Government to change the plan. The document states that the dredging of the town river will obstruct the residents' houses, and they request that the government adopt a plan that protects property rights and maintains the people's livelihood. Meng Hua and others are citizens of the Lixing District of this city and have lived in Lixing Town for generations. Some have established shops, and others are residences. In the past few years, the river channel of the East and West Zhu Family Gully in this township was silted up, and the irrigation of farmland was at stake. The citizens proposed dredging, and because the situation in each township was different, they presented the various obstacles to the Municipal Government's Public Works Bureau and the Lixing District Municipal Committee Office, requesting a detailed discussion and cautious implementation. The Municipal Government clearly ordered that the section of the town's river be dredged together with the East and West Zhu Family Gully. This should be complied with. Regarding the request to build dams at the river mouth where the East and West Zhu Family Gully connect to the Dutai River, officials should be sent to investigate the actual situation before further review. The superiors were very considerate of the people's difficulties. However, the Zhu Family Gully has been silted up for a long time. Although dredging is necessary, it is necessary to dredge the trunk rivers such as the Ma Family River and Dutai River first to achieve the effect of connecting the trunk and branches. Recently, the old matter has been brought up again, and the previous proposal has been reiterated. Meng Hua and others have a vital stake and cannot remain silent. They respectfully present their views to the Municipal Government in detail. The Zhu Family Gully is divided into two streams, east and west, passing through figures 4, 5, 6, 38, and 44, with a length of seven miles. Figure 6 accounts for three-quarters of the length and is more closely related. The rising tide of the West Zhu Family River flows in from the Ma Family Hong River, and its discharge must also pass through the Ma Family Hong River mouth. This is because its downward flow is lower and faster than the meandering Dutai River, which flows far and slowly. It is impossible to compare the two. Dredging the West Zhu Family Gully to connect to the Ma Family Hong River is sufficient to accommodate the ebb and flow of the tide. The East Zhu Family Gully is connected to the Yunyan River in the east, directly reaching Hangzhou. The source is large and the circulation is fast, so there is no problem for discharge. However, the Zhu Family Gully is not suitable for navigation and can only be used for farmland irrigation. But farmland irrigation is suitable for clean water and not tidal water. Anyone with a little knowledge of agriculture can know this. If we still hold the previous proposal to dredge the town's river together, the tide will invade with fierce force, and the amount of sediment carried in will be even greater. Not only will we repeat the situation of the Zhuang Family Gully near the river being dredged and silted up three times every ten years, but also the internal tributaries will be silted up and become dry. This will cause the families that use it for farmland irrigation to be cut off from the source of drinking water for the residents. Dredging again and again will be endless, and our people will be exhausted and have no time to breathe. This is the first disadvantage of dredging the Zhu Family Gully and the town's river together. Also, the section of the Zhu Family Gully's town river is an important market town in Lixing Town. The small shops of hundreds of households will inevitably be demolished and have no way to survive. Even if the width is reduced and construction and dredging are carried out, the foundation of the houses on both sides will inevitably be loosened and collapse. At a time when rural commerce is declining, there is no such financial resources to seek another way to make a living. It is tantamount to sacrificing the lives and property of hundreds of households to dredge the town's river and destroying the market town, causing the residents to be displaced and forever sinking into an irrecoverable abyss. Although the citizens are foolish, at this critical juncture of life and death, they will certainly rise up and resist, and they will never be willing to submit. If this leads to an accident, who will take the blame? This is the second disadvantage of dredging the Zhu Family Gully and the town's river together. Looking at the history of the town's river, there is the Sen Yutang, Chengyi Tang, Yixun Tang, and Yinxiang Caotang in the south of the river, and the Tao Shen family's memorial arch for filial piety in the north of the river. These were all constructed during the Qianlong and Jiaqing periods of the Former Qing Dynasty, and their ruins still exist today. This can serve as ironclad proof that the town's river cannot be easily dredged. Also, the two dredgings of the Zhu Family Gully in the 52nd year before the founding of the Republic of China and in the 6th year of the Republic of China both started from the Ma Family Hong River mouth and ended at the Little Wooden Bridge west of the town. The facts are available and can be easily investigated. This is the third disadvantage of dredging the Zhu Family Gully and the town's river together. As far as our humble opinions are concerned, we propose to dredge from the Ma Family Hong River mouth of the West Zhu Family Gully to the Little Wooden Bridge west of Lixing Town, and the East Zhu Family Gully from the Qifeng Bridge east of the town to the Xiantang River. A dam and sluice gate should be built at the Ma Family Hong River mouth in the West Zhu Family Gully to avoid the disadvantages of rising tide and siltation. The East Mi Family Gully has a long flow and a clean source, and there is no risk of siltation. This is the first advantage. Also, the built sluice gate can be opened and closed at any time, which is also a help in preventing drought and floods. Moreover, the sluice gate closes the water and cleans the river bottom silt, water plants, and other things, which are rich in fertilizer for the fields, making the river channel deeper and deeper, so our people can benefit once and for all. This is several advantages in one fell swoop. This is the second advantage. The silted areas of the town's river should be filled with soil to expand the streets in the future and maintain the prosperity of land transportation, which is beneficial to the market. This is the second advantage. Looking at the matter of building dams, such as the Wang Family Gully in figures 17 and 18 of this district, the original tidal tributary river channel had already been silted up. Therefore, construction began six years ago to dredge it. After dredging, a dam was built to change the tidal river into a clean water river. Today, the river channel of the gully is in good condition, and irrigation is convenient. This is the benefit of building a dam, there is an example to follow, and it is easy to investigate and obtain. In short, comparing the above-mentioned advantages and disadvantages, the citizens cannot agree to the proposal to dredge the Zhu Family Gully and the town's river together. If only the West Zhu Family Gully is dredged to the Little Wooden Bridge west of the town, and the East Zhu Family Gully to the Qifeng Bridge east of the town, and a sluice gate is set up at the Ma Family Hong River mouth, all the citizens will be happy to see it happen. This matter is related to the irrigation of the entire river and the interests of all the residents of the town. The livelihoods of Meng Hua and others are at stake, and they cannot sit idly by. Therefore, we dare not presume to present our humble views and recommend Tao Menghua, Tao Qinwen, Tao Hongcan, and Zhang Zhenqi as representatives to present the details in person. We respectfully request the Municipal Government to follow public opinion, approve the adoption of our proposal, and earnestly request that the section of the town's river be exempted from dredging before the plan is approved by public opinion. We respectfully beg for approval, and we will await orders with the utmost anxiety. Respectfully submitted to Wu, the Mayor of Shanghai. Submitters: Tao Menghua and 72 others.

Li Guocheng's Sentence Reduced After Two Appeals to the Supreme Court and Retrial. Original Sentence of Life Imprisonment Reduced to Twelve Years. Li Still Unhappy, Plans to Appeal Again. 166

On the evening of August 13, the 20th year of the Republic of China, a case occurred in the Fashang Hotel on Xinxinqiao Street in the French Concession where Jiangbei bandits brutally killed their comrades, Jiang Zhonghan, Xia Yongsheng, and a Xue surname person, and wounded Zhong Ziqing. The French Police apprehended the culprit, Yan Jinbiao, a native of Funing, on the spot. After prosecution, the Second Special Court sentenced him to death. The sentence was affirmed after three trials and executed according to law. During the interrogation, Yan confessed that the ringleader was his fellow townsman, Li Guocheng, also known as Chen Youliang. Li was handed over to the Public Security Bureau by Yan's family in Rihui Port. After being brought back by the Second Special Court for the initial trial, he was sentenced to death. He appealed to the High Court Three Branch, but the result was rejected. He appealed again to the Supreme Court, which sent the case back for retrial and changed the sentence to life imprisonment. Li was still dissatisfied, and his father filed an appeal with the Supreme Court for a retrial. Now, the reasons for the retrial have been sent back, stating that the case had undergone a general amnesty, which the original trial had not taken into account. The High Court Three Branch held a retrial and concluded the case the other day. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the court ruled to revoke the original judgment and sentenced Li Guocheng to twelve years of imprisonment for joint murder. After the verdict, he was sent back to the detention center. It is said that after Li left the court, he told his defense lawyer and family that he did not participate in the murder and was still being wrongly sentenced. He would never be willing to accept this and would file another appeal after receiving the judgment. This case has been going on for more than five years now. The Supreme Court has twice decided to send the case back for retrial. Li believes that he must be acquitted to be satisfied.

Page 16

Renting School Premises: Opening a Casino at Night. "Cifanhheshang" and Others Thinking Wishfully. Many Arrested After Police Investigation. 167

Fan Rongxi, a well-known gangster nicknamed "Cifanhheshang" (Rice Porridge Monk), and Yang Lansheng, nicknamed "Mapilansheng" (Pockmarked Lansheng), recently opened mobile gambling tables in the Dongyang Wharf area. Because the police authorities were strictly arresting them, they found it difficult to gain a foothold and had to relocate. The premises of a certain school at No. 28, Lane 411, Dagu Road, are owned by Li Jichang. The school has no classes at night. Fan and Yang took advantage of this opportunity to discuss with Li and temporarily set up a gambling place in the school. Every night, they called out numbers and gambled all night long. There were often as many as fifty or sixty gamblers. The Chengdu Road Police Station's Chinese Detective Feng Baishun and detectives Wang Yongjun, Xu Dezhong, and Sun Wenxi discovered this. Because they had good sources of information and there were many people, they were afraid of missing someone. Therefore, at 9:30 PM the other night, they dispatched additional detectives Chen Yaoting, Zhou Yushan, and Bao Detective Zhang Kui to the area and surrounded it. They immediately arrested the gamblers. At that time, they arrested forty-one gamblers, including Yang Ruisheng, Zhou Ajin, Hu Jinsheng, Cai Acheng, Wang San, Zhang Liangen, Zhang Xingsheng, Xue Xuyuan, Monk Zhu, Wang Zhaoxi, Wang Fusheng, Wang Arong, Liu Xianglin, Wang Xuqing, Chen Mulin, Gao Arong, Xia Youtang, Ni Shijin, Chen Adong, and Gu Xiaofeng, Sun Wenpu. Fan and Yang, the two ringleaders, had already escaped. They took all the gambling equipment back to the police station. Except for fifteen who were each allowed to post 100 yuan bail, the rest were detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police station lawyer, Qian Xunhua, filed a gambling charge and said that the landlord, Li Jichang, would be appropriately punished. After questioning by Judge Ye Shengchao one by one, it was ruled that those who posted bail would be fined 40 yuan each, and the rest would be fined 15 yuan each.

Labor Dispute Resolved 168

Baohua and Yiyou Factories

The Caojiadu Binhua Yiyou Yucun Silk Factory had a strike because dismissed workers were ordered to be reinstated but were rejected by the management. Because the current situation is tense and the labor unrest cannot be delayed, the Municipal Party Department, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the General Labor Union convened a mediation meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday, led by Lu Jingshi, a member of the Municipal Party Department. Zhang Chuqiang from the Social Affairs Bureau, Yi Tiegeng from the General Labor Union, labor representatives Jin Xiuwen, Wang Xiuzhen, Xing Xiaolin, Huang Chengyun, Huang Heqin, Zhou Genyuan, and management representatives Yu Xiting from Baohua Factory and Wu Weinong from Yiyou Factory attended. Committee Member Lu explained the situation to the management, and after two hours of discussion, a mediation agreement was reached. The methods are listed below: (1) Baohua Factory: 1. In accordance with the Social Affairs Bureau's instructions, workers Zhang Baixi and Zhang Yuezhen are allowed to be reinstated. 2. Each dismissed worker will be given two months' severance pay, calculated at 20 yuan for those with monthly wages below 20 yuan, 20 yuan for those with wages between 20 and 30 yuan, and the actual wage for those above 30 yuan. 3. The factory will consider compensating for the losses suffered by each dismissed worker during the work stoppage. (2) Yiyou Factory: 1. In accordance with the Social Affairs Bureau's instructions, all dismissed workers will be reinstated. If the factory finds that the workers are not skilled with the flower weaving machines, they may be given ten days to learn. During the learning period, they will be given four jiao per day. 2. If the workers are still not skilled after ten days, the factory may stop their learning, and at the same time, the factory must be responsible for introducing them to a new job. Before obtaining a job, daily meal money will be paid as usual. 3. The factory will consider compensating for the losses suffered by each dismissed worker during the work stoppage. (3) In the future, factories shall not dismiss workers without reason. (4) Workers of both Baohua and Yiyou factories shall resume work on the morning of December 16. The agreement was signed by representatives of all parties. As for the Yuli Silk Factory, which had unreasonably dismissed workers, violated government orders, and refused to accept mediation by the Municipal Party Department, it is said that the Municipal Party Department plans to ask the government to impose sanctions during this period of serious situation to quell the labor unrest and prevent cunning and stubbornness.

China Match Factory

The China Match Factory at Pingjiang Bridge in Zhabei has been experiencing a labor dispute for a month. The labor side has repeatedly petitioned the Municipal Party Department, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the General Labor Union for mediation. The General Labor Union sent specialist Wan Banghe to convene both sides for negotiations twice, and a mediation agreement was reached yesterday. The resolution of the General Labor Union is recorded below: The China Match Company violated the Factory Law, and the resolution determined by the union is as follows: (1) The original requests for working ten hours per month and for no arbitrary dismissal of workers will be reserved for discussion after January. (2) Unless there are more than 1,200 boxes of inventory or the machines and buildings are damaged and need to be repaired, if work is stopped, the factory shall provide workers with two jiao for meals per day (male workers). (3) Child labor shall work the same hours as adult labor. (4) Government-stipulated commemorative days shall be handled in accordance with the law. (5) Female workers shall be granted leave for childbirth and shall be paid three yuan in wages. Children shall not be brought into the factory except for breastfeeding, except during work stoppages. (6) If there is a surplus at the end of the year, bonuses shall be paid. (7) If a worker is injured on duty, the factory shall provide a certificate from a designated hospital or doctor and pay for medical expenses in addition to providing leave. During the leave, two jiao shall be provided for meals per day. (8) For the three weeks of the recent work stoppage, except for the previous two weeks that both parties agreed not to count, for the remaining eight days, the factory shall pay male workers two jiao for meals per day. (9) This resolution shall take effect from the date of signature by both parties. December 14, 25th year of the Republic of China. Labor representatives Jiang Yuncai (signed), Gu Xinkun (signed), Tang Ayi (signed), Sun Haishan (signed), Management representatives Pan Guiru (signed), Ye Fuqiao (signed), Undertaker Wan Banghe (stamped), Recorder Fang Rusheng (stamped).

Yarn and Cloth Exchange: Announcement of Trading Limits 170

Effective Today

The Yarn and Cloth Exchange market revealed Announcement No. 1971, which stated that it was issued under Order No. 48968 of the Ministry of Industry, regarding the restrictions on the amount of futures trading. It is recorded as follows: (1) The remaining balance of futures trading for each broker in each month is limited to 5,000 pieces of cotton yarn and 20,000 dan of cotton. (2) If the limit is exceeded, for cotton yarn from 5,050 to 10,000 pieces, and for cotton from 20,100 to 30,000 dan, in addition to the margin deposit, cotton should be paid at 10% of the registered price and cotton yarn at 5%, which cannot be substituted, and a special margin deposit should be added according to the amount of the margin deposit paid, which also cannot be substituted. (3) If the trading volume of cotton yarn is more than 10,000 pieces, increasing every 5,000 pieces, and the trading volume of cotton is more than 30,000 dan, increasing every 10,000 dan, the special margin deposit will be doubled and cannot be substituted. The right to implement the above orders will be followed uniformly from the 16th. In addition to notifying the Brokerage Association, this is hereby announced.

Robbery and Injury on Gonghe Road 172

The home of Tang Guoshun, a Taizhou native who manages the parcel room at the Postal Administration, is located at No. 37 at the end of Lane 4, Hexingli, Gonghe Road, Zhabei. It is a single-room shikumen house. Tang himself lives in the back of the downstairs parlor, while the upstairs front building and the garret are rented out, and the back building is currently vacant. Unexpectedly, at around 7 pm the night before, Tang went to his relative's house for some business. Tang's wife was having dinner with the children when she suddenly heard someone knocking on the door. Tang's wife immediately went to open the door. The bandits claimed that they were going to see a friend in the garret. After entering the door, the bandits showed a pistol. Tang's wife knew that they were robbers, so she rushed into the room and closed the door tightly. The bandits then entered through the wall and pressed Tang's wife to the ground, and used the pistol butt to hit her head, hands, and feet, forcing her to reveal the location of the hidden money. As a result, 110 yuan in legal tender belonging to Tang's relatives in the suitcase was robbed. Tang Guoshun's own 200 yuan in legal tender, 8 silver dollars, a gold bracelet, four rings, two spare buttons, men's and women's coats, raincoats, cheongsams, silver ornaments, etc., were robbed, worth about 700 yuan. The strangest thing is that when the bandits finished robbing and were about to leave, they were afraid that Tang's wife would go out and shout for help, so they brought a padlock to lock the door leading from the ladder down to the stove surface. All the raincoats and robes were worn away by the bandits, because it was raining at the time. Yesterday, Tang's wife's head and face were swollen, and she was seriously injured. Tang's wife said that everything in the room, except for the chamber pot, was ransacked by the bandits. Two pillows on the bed were also torn open, so the room was very messy. Yesterday, the victim has submitted a list to the police station in charge to investigate the stolen goods.

Attempted Murder: Xu Yongcai Sentenced 173

Chi Wenxiang, a man from Pudong and the son-in-law of a wealthy Wei family living on Gordon Road, is over forty years old and works in a paint shop. On the evening of September 14 this year, his cousin Xia Boliang tricked Chi into a pre-rented garret at No. 38, Tongkangli, Avenue Notre Dame, in the French Concession under the pretext of contacting business, and let Chi stay overnight. That night, he colluded with Xu Afu and Xu Yongcai to try to kill Chi with knives. Fortunately, Chi was strong and resisted and shouted for help, and the murderers escaped. Chi was seriously injured. The police pursued and captured one of the murderers, Xu Yongcai, and escorted him to the Special Second Court for interrogation and detention. Chi was sent to the hospital for treatment. The French Police Department filed a public prosecution against Xu Yongcai for attempted murder. After interrogation by Judge Zhang Chaozuo, the case was adjourned for further investigation. Judge Yi was transferred to the Jiangxi High Court, and Judge Sun Penghuan took over the case. After several court hearings and investigation of evidence, Judge Sun of the First Criminal Court sentenced Xu Yongcai yesterday morning to seven years of imprisonment for attempted murder, with deprivation of public rights for five years. After the sentence, the defendant was transferred back to the detention center.

Boy Crushed to Death by Car 174

The boy, Cao Miaode, seven years old, lived at No. 80, Jinxiuli, Xiangjie Lu, Yudaikou. At around 6 pm yesterday, he was walking past the intersection of Xinzha Road and Dalu Road when he was knocked down by a No. 15003 Route 10 public bus. The wheels crushed his head severely. Later, Hua Police No. 2983 saw him and sent him to Tongren Hospital in an ambulance. Due to his severe injuries, he died before arriving at the hospital.

Publishing Industry 175

The China Economic Yearbook is published by Shiwai Publishing House, No. 230, Benpu Road. In view of the current efforts of our government to promote the National Economic Construction Movement, it is urgent to have detailed investigations and accurate statistics on the organization and current situation of the economy in various parts of the country in order to improve the facts and circumstances and serve as a guide for improvement. The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated that Shandong and the Yellow River basin are cloudy and cold, and there may be snowfall. There will be northeast to southwest winds. The middle and upper reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with rain or fog and northeast to northwest winds. New Transportation Promotion Association Passes the Implementation Measures for Inland River Ferry New Transportation; Decides to Notify Relevant Agencies and Groups to Take Charge of Implementation; General Association and Ministry of Transportation Will Send Personnel to Inspect and Assess 179

The New Life Movement Promotion Association of this city, in order to implement the new inland river navigation and transportation measures, convened a joint meeting of relevant agencies and groups at the conference hall of the Fenglinqiao Municipal Party Headquarters at 10 am yesterday, which passed the implementation measures. Details are recorded below:

Joint Meeting

The New Transportation Promotion Association convened a joint meeting of relevant agencies and groups at 10 am yesterday. More than a dozen people attended, including Li Shangbin of the Navigation Administration, Dong Zhenkang of the China Seafarers Inland River Office, Gao Shuan of the Public Works Bureau, Xie Yisheng of the Public Security Bureau, Jian Ping of the Inland River Transfer Boat Association, and Jiang Hao of the New Transportation Promotion Association. Jiang Hao chaired the meeting, and Zhu Jiarang recorded the minutes. The chairman reported that he was ordered to promote the new navigation transportation measures. Then, the agencies released information on the pier equipment, personnel management, and travel measures. At the end, they discussed (1) the draft of the measures to promote the new inland river navigation and transportation measures, and decided to pass it; (2) the proposal to determine the start date, and decided to implement it yesterday; (3) the proposal to have the New Transportation Association notify the relevant agencies and groups to be responsible for implementation, and decided to pass it.

Implementation Measures

The implementation measures for the new inland river navigation and transportation passed are as follows: 1. Scope: All inland river ferry ships must use these measures to promote the new transportation. 2. Items: (1) Pier: (1) Equipment: 1. Install boarding bridges and mark the words "up" and "down". 2. Install life-saving equipment and waiting equipment. 3. The pier stone steps or slopes must be repaired and leveled, and cleaned at least once a day. 4. The pontoon boats must be cleaned at least once a day. 5. Set up a lost and found sign in the most conspicuous place for traffic. (2) Personnel: 1. Passengers must line up in order when purchasing and getting on and off the ship. 2. Passengers' clothes must be neat and tidy. 3. Porters must wear uniforms. 4. Idle people are prohibited from lingering. 5. Porters are prohibited from fighting and noisy. (2) Ferry Ship: (1) Equipment: 1. Install life-saving equipment. 2. Install fire-fighting equipment. 3. Install medicines for epidemic prevention and seasickness. 4. The berths must be repaired and leveled and must be cleaned at least once a day. 5. The kitchen must be cleaned at least once a day. 6. The toilets must be flushed at least once a day. 7. A public tea drinking place must be set up in a traffic artery or open space, and it must be kept clean at all times. 8. The sides of the passenger cabin must be washed at least once a day. 9. A lost and found column must be set up in a conspicuous place in a traffic artery. 10. Entertainment equipment and books must be set up. 11. If the ship is damaged and cannot maintain a safe state, it should stop running immediately and be repaired immediately. 12. Set up an opinion box to collect opinions from passengers. 2. Personnel: (1) Ship staff: 1. The attitude must be dignified, the uniform must be neat and tidy, and the treatment of people must be kind. 2. You must be kind and courteous and persuade passengers to fulfill the regulations. (3) The fare must be fair and honest and no extra points should be collected. 4. Unboiled water must not be provided for passengers to drink. 5. Idle people and singers must be prohibited from boarding the ship. 6. Bowls, teacups, etc. must be washed after use. 7. If you encounter the elderly, children, and women, etc., 8. You must take care of and protect them. 8. Tea must be charged according to the set price and no extra points should be solicited. 5. Porters must wear uniforms. 7. Porters must wait for the passenger to disembark before engaging in loading and unloading. 11. Porters must prepare number plates to be handed over to passengers for safekeeping, so that passengers can pick up their belongings with the plates. (2) Passengers: 1. The clothes must be neat and clean. 2. Line up in order when purchasing tickets and getting on and off the ship. 3. Give way to the elderly, children, and women first and take care of them. 4. You must stop getting on and off the ship when the ship is moving. 5. Do not spit or urinate anywhere. 6. The equipment on the ship must be carefully protected and kept clean. 7. Be polite and humble to the ship staff and fellow passengers, do not quarrel, and accept advice. 8. You must purchase tickets in accordance with the regulations, and do not quarrel rudely. 9. You must not smoke opium and gamble in public. 10. Do not cross the boundaries of your seat or berth. Next, 1. If you have any suggestions or opinions, please write them clearly and put them in the opinion box. 12. You must pay attention to fire and check your belongings at any time. 13. Passengers must get on first and then get off. Three Steps (1) Convene a meeting. The Mountain New Transportation General Association or local New Transportation Associations will work with the transportation authorities to send personnel to convene the following agencies to discuss matters of progress: 1. The shipping industry union, 2. Shipping company, 3. Police agencies, 4. Military police agencies, 5. Military agencies, 6. Ship inspection agencies. If there is no New Transportation Association organization in the inland area, the shipping industry union will be responsible for convening discussions and proceeding. (2) Implementation: 1. Shen Bao National Goods Special Issue

My Interview Experience 180

— Interviewer — Xu Songzi

In the cold wind, we were battling. From countless roads to obscure alleyways, it almost felt like the more we walked, the colder and more desolate it became, with only the rickshaw pullers' footsteps accompanying our own heartbeats.

It was already deep winter!

But the cold wind could not chill our passion for working for national products, nor could it chill the patriotic conscience of the giant that Chinese women are. Isn't it so? Who can say that our household interview work isn't expanding and deepening with the passage of time? Who can say that wise housewives are not deeply moved and standing on the front lines of economic national defense?

The past three months of interview work have not been in vain. But in order to strengthen the national products movement and share some of my foolish insights from my work experience, it is not without meaning, right?

1. The Technique of Entering the Door

If we are conducting interviews in the morning, please remember not to knock on the front door. This is a common situation in Shanghai. Because in the morning, almost all housewives or maids are busy preparing lunch in the kitchen behind the house; they are so busy that who has time to open the front door?

In the afternoon, it's completely the opposite. Then you can boldly ring the doorbell at the front door or knock on the knocker. That's when most families are working or resting in the living room!

2. A Timid Person is a Failed Person

Why should we "boldly" ring the doorbell or knock on the knocker? Because a timid person is a failed person!

Just think: if you ring or knock softly, will the people inside hear you? Even if they do hear you, judging by your timid manner, wouldn't the maid take you for a stranger? In this day and age, everyone is wary of strangers! When you are given the cold shoulder, would you hate the maid or hate yourself? Therefore, we must be bolder! Not only that, when the maid asks who it is from behind the door, you must answer kindly and loudly, as if you were a close relative or friend of the family. Naturally, they will open the door for you.

3. How to Request an Audience with the Housewife?

The door is open. How to request an audience with the housewife? This cannot be generalized. There are many methods. First, you must remind yourself at this moment to be more intelligent, that is, to "adapt to the situation." For example, if you are in a household with a high level of education, it is appropriate to use our particularly large card. After the card is sent in, it will be welcomed by the housewife. Otherwise, that large card may be a bit intimidating. Another approach is to present some fabric samples. Those colorful books of fabric samples are very appealing. If you have the opportunity to explain your intentions to the maid, that would be even better.

4. Seize Every Opportunity

Again, "adapting to the situation" is extremely important in interview work. Needless to say, if you see the housewife and notice that she has one or more children with her, you should start by talking about the children. If she is knitting with wool in her hands, you should discuss knitting patterns. This way, when the conversation becomes engaging, you can proceed to discuss national products, and the result will be universally beneficial. Not only that, for example, if you have entered someone's house, you can take advantage of someone who has just walked into the house and talk to them, which can invisibly help you overcome the difficulty of entering the house. Similarly, asking one or two children playing on the street or in the alley to lead you back to their home is also a good method. As for enthusiastic housewives who are willing to introduce you to acquaintances, it is an even greater success.

5. Standing Before Proud Housewives

Naturally, most housewives are very receptive to our opinions. But standing before proud housewives is quite difficult to handle. At that time, you must generally say the following words to her humbly:

"My visit to your home this time is very presumptuous. There is also a belief behind bothering ladies like this, which is to work for national products. In order to make national products improve day by day, we must come to families and listen to the insightful opinions of ladies who are knowledgeable, experienced, and enthusiastically patriotic…"

Few people would not be moved by such words.

6. How to Persuade Housewives with Limited Views?

"Promoting national products is an effective way to save the national economic crisis."

"Using national products is the natural duty of citizens." Slogans like these will lose their power to stimulate in the ears of housewives with limited views.

We need to make the slogans a bit more grounded. For example, say to her, "When Chinese people use Chinese goods, Chinese money can only be earned by Chinese people. If we buy foreign goods, isn't Chinese money being earned by foreigners?" Or, for example, "Two brothers, the Wang brothers. If the older brother's money is used by the younger brother, it is always used by people in the family. If it is used by Zhang San and Li Si, how can that be?" This kind of clever saying naturally has a great effect!

Interview Notes

An Interview with Mr. Chen Shoufeng 181

— Jiang Xia

It was through the introduction of my friend Mr. Wang that I got to know Mr. Chen Shoufeng. If Mr. Wang hadn't explained, who would believe that such a young and solid person is actually an industrialist who has founded more than a dozen industries? After a round of pleasantries, our conversation began:

"Mr. Chen, could you tell me about your motivation for founding a silk weaving business?" I asked.

"Hmm, the silk industry! No one would believe it, but I originally had no roots in the silk industry at all. The reason for founding it was that the Xiangchang Silk Factory, founded by my father's friend, Mr. Shi Shaochu, was not performing well and urgently needed someone to reorganize it. He repeatedly invited me to take on the position. At first, I was a bit apprehensive, but later I made up my mind with the principle that 'as long as I work hard, I won't be afraid of failure,' and I dared to accept the position of manager. Although I lost more than ten thousand yuan in the first year, by April and May of the following year, I had already earned back what I had lost, and the scope of the factory gradually expanded, and the capital also increased from fifty thousand yuan to one million yuan. Later, the output really couldn't meet the demand, so I decided on a material distribution system, but I didn't expect it would lead to the current situation of 'one factory every few steps.'" After saying this, he took a puff of smoke and smiled.

"What kind of businesses did Mr. Chen run before running the silk factory?"

"The dyeing and weaving factory and the toothbrush factory were both founded when I was around twenty years old. Later, I once cooperated with Mr. Liu Guojun in the dyeing and weaving business, but soon Mr. Liu went to Changzhou to open a yarn factory and had no time to take care of it, so the partnership dissolved implicitly. However, the factory still exists today."

"The toothbrush business is still an emerging industry in China, right?"

"Yes, when I founded the Zhenyu Toothbrush Factory, it was one of the only ones in China. At that time, I saw foreign toothbrushes flooding our country's market, and I aspired to establish a toothbrush factory. After more than a year of preparation, and with the strong support of my father, I was able to establish it. Although I lost more than 50,000 yuan in the short term, I felt very happy in spirit that foreign goods had disappeared. As for the fact that the toothbrush manufacturing industry has now become a small household industry, I never would have thought of it when I first started."

"Mr. Chen, what are your opinions on running a glass business?"

"Hmm, that is very difficult to do. Take the Zhongshan Glass Factory, which I closed down last year, as an example. The business was very prosperous. Glass cups alone sold more than a thousand dozens a day. However, the workers' lack of knowledge prevented them from connecting with the factory, and it ultimately failed. Therefore, the lack of universal education is indeed very dangerous for the future of industry." Mr. Chen said unhappily.

Mr. Chen's eloquence was very strong, and he became more energetic as he spoke. Before I knew it, we had been talking for more than a quarter of an hour. There were already two people waiting to discuss matters, so I bid farewell and left.

The Future of National Product Development 182

— Xuan Wan

Recently, our national product industry has developed greatly. There is no doubt that this is indeed a fact. The production and sales of domestic products from January to July of this year—its sales volume has increased by more than one-third compared with the same period last year. At the same time, Chinese National Products Companies have been established in various places. Now there are as many as twelve, spread throughout the major cities of the country, gradually forming a network of national production and sales cooperation. This good phenomenon, on the one hand, demonstrates the upsurge of the national products movement, which has now gained the love of the vast majority of people in the country, and on the other hand, it demonstrates even more that it has laid the most solid foundation for the future of the entire national economic construction movement.

Although, at present, we should make a new estimate and a new review of the overall development prospects of national products. We need to know the reasons for the recent increase in sales of domestic products. What problems are still hindering its future? This is something that everyone engaged in national products should understand, as it is very necessary to develop future work.

Here, I think anyone with a slight understanding of the future of national products can immediately understand that the main reasons for the progress of national products this year are, first, the low domestic exchange rates and good harvests in various places, which promoted the increase in people's purchasing power, and second, the national product manufacturers' own efforts to promote sales, prices lower than foreign goods, and active promotion to Guangdong, Sichuan, and the Northwest. However, the biggest obstacle to its future is the obstruction of smuggling. Recently, there have been rumors that North China will levy a special tax on smuggled goods (only one-eighth of the customs duty), which will allow smuggled goods to openly and actively enter the domestic market. This is really a matter of life and death for our entire national product industry. We hope that it is not true, otherwise we will fight for it based on reason in order to find a solution.

Regarding the future development of national products, we must also strive for (1) progress in domestic transportation construction, so that national products can be easily transported and sold inland, (2) hope that the local authorities will abolish various special taxes that hinder the development of national products, so as to reduce the burden, and (3) should sincerely cooperate with overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia to open up overseas markets, so that national products can advance overseas.

In short, the future development of national products is very promising, as long as we all work harder in the future!

Brief news: The Zhengtai Xinji Rubber Factory in this city previously misused the name "Wanli Shoes" of the factory for industrial rubber, and sued according to the law. Later, through the mediation of Mr. Zhang Chuqiang and Mr. Wang Gongxian, it has come to an end, and the factory also, out of industry relations, could not bear to be harsh, and did not care about the losses suffered. Now the industrial factory, at the request of Zhengtai Factory, specially donated 200 yuan in legal currency to the museum for remittance to the anti-Japanese soldiers in Sui Province, to express condolences and encourage Chinese people.

Announcement: This journal will print a "Toy Special Issue" in the next issue, soliciting articles on children's toys, each article limited to 500 characters, and must be sent within five days.

Contribution

Production and Sales Should Correspond 184

— Yang An

The failure of Chinese national product factories lies not in the dumping of foreign goods, but in the infighting among the same industry. For a certain product, it is clear that there is already a factory whose products are sufficient to meet the demand, but those who covet its profit, not knowing the importance, and without self-assessment, set up another factory to compete with it. For example, for a certain national product, the annual sales are 5 million yuan, and the existing factories have more than 5 million yuan of production, and there is already a feeling of oversupply, but a new force suddenly rises, and someone sets up another factory to join the competition. As a result, the newly established factory will inevitably suffer a miserable defeat, and the original factory, without exception, will still have lingering fears. Therefore, I often wish that national product factories should pay close attention to the overall problem, and there should be a method to consider the overall situation. And entrepreneurs who want to set up new factories should also carefully examine the pros and cons, and invest cautiously, and not just take a temporary small profit as a profit. Recently, the Minfeng Paper Factory, in order to count the current situation of domestic cigarette paper production and sales, advised the national entrepreneurs to invest cautiously. This matter is very much in line with our original intention, and is indeed a proof of the progress of the national product industry. At present, for cigarette paper production, the Minfeng Factory alone, if two machines are fully opened, has more than 840,000 rolls per year, while the domestic demand, including foreign merchants, is at most 740,000 rolls, which has become slightly surplus. According to this situation, cigarette paper production is sufficient to be self-sufficient. If a new factory is set up, the oversupply will be too much, and it will inevitably lead to a drop in prices and dumping, harming others and harming oneself. Rather than perish together, why not seek another way? There are many industries that should be run domestically, why must you go to the nationally produced products that have already been run by people and feel that they are oversupplied, to disrupt the market and bring about failure? There are many paths for my country's production industry, and we can examine the state of demand from the standpoint of the overall national economy, and carefully invest in the direction, and strive to make running an industry benefit the country, benefit the people, and make the society prosperous, and foreign goods will also disappear from this. Each additional factory like this will strengthen the country's strength and increase the vitality of society. In a nutshell: it is not difficult to start, but it lies in the ability to "correspond production and sales to suit supply and demand."

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 185

— (Xu Xiaoting)

Talent is a bright and lustrous jade tablet, which needs to be ground and carved, and then nurtured with knowledge, so that talent can be used by people.

To unleash the greatness of talent, it is necessary to instill considerable knowledge to guide talent, and to strengthen the richness of knowledge, it is necessary to study considerable learning to develop talent.

The Analects of Confucius says: Hui could know ten things from hearing one, and Si could know two things from hearing one. The extent of talent in raising one and reversing one, and raising one and grasping three, can be derived from here as a touchstone.

The pouring of spring water must have a smooth flowing river channel, and the cultivation of talents must have a beautiful and good education. A long-stored mirror needs to be wiped to be bright, and a long-hidden moon needs to have the veil swept away to be dazzling.

Talent will sometimes automatically flow outward, but automatic leakage is easy to run into the wrong path, and passive guidance will go on the right track.

Look at Chinese society, there are too many people being eroded, one is due to improper use, and the other is due to improper use of talent. The obstruction and stagnation of social undertakings are indeed due to the fact that the volatility of talent comes too immature and decadent.

The Daughter in the Ji Family Inn 186

— Zhou Bao

In the eleventh year of the Republic of China—I, with my aunt and uncle, went from Bozhou, Anhui, to South Suzhou, taking the Jinpu train back to Jiangsu. On the way from Bozhou to Suzhou, we suddenly heard that there was a bandit alarm thirty miles ahead, so we had to stay in Qinglugou, a place bordering Jiangsu and Anhui. It was the only Ji Family Inn. Needless to say, the equipment was simple. At that time, we originally planned to stay for one night and leave, but the bandits ahead were fighting each other day after day, so we had to spend day after day at the Ji Family Inn. After enduring until the fifth day, in the early morning, there was a commotion in the backyard. My aunt was awakened from her sleep. Suddenly she could not find my uncle, so she ran to the next room to look for him. I hurriedly got up, put on my clothes, and went to the backyard, only to see my uncle and a girl tied back-to-back, placed on the kang. I knew that girl, she was the daughter of the Ji Family Inn. Although her skin was quite fair, and her feet were quite small (at that time, in the rural areas there, women still regarded small feet as beautiful), but those cross-eyes had already caught my attention on the first day.

At that time, five burly men were standing in front of the kang, menacingly, trying to send my uncle to the authorities, saying that he had sexually assaulted a maiden. Later, they learned about my relationship with my uncle, so they turned around and threatened me. At that time, I was so frightened that I was stunned and didn't know what to do. In the end, it was still my uncle who negotiated with them himself, settled it with forty-six strings of cash, and regained his freedom. Coincidentally, that day at noon, the old rickshaw puller said that it was already calm ahead, so we left the Ji Family Inn in a disheveled state. When the cart pulled out of Qinglugou, the five burly men who had been seen in the morning, their faces flushed from drinking, came towards us. The old rickshaw puller laughed and said, "You made a good deal." One of them replied, "What a good deal, our five brothers only got a net of eight strings of cash." After the five men passed, the old rickshaw puller, with intermittent sentences, told us that the daughter in the Ji Family Inn only did these "honey trap" stories. So all the way, my uncle was scolded by my aunt until they reached Suzhou.

Less than five years after returning to the village, my aunt and uncle passed away one after another. This farcical drama also gradually dissipated in my mind like smoke. Unexpectedly, in the past month, a family pulling a rickety cart moved into the bungalow opposite my Shanghai residence. One day, I suddenly heard my maid chatting with the woman from that family, and the woman said that she was from Qinglugou, Anhui. My heart fluttered, I looked carefully, the outline was vaguely familiar, and those cross-eyes were still unharmed. So I couldn't help but exclaimed, "You are the daughter in the Ji Family Inn." Hearing this, her face flushed, and she walked away pretending not to hear. From then on, when she saw me, she avoided me from afar. Last week, she moved away silently.

More than ten years have passed, and she has aged so much that she doesn't look like a middle-aged woman, and she is already the mother of five children. But how did she drift into this city? This is a mystery, perhaps it will never be known to me.

Street Manufacturers 187

— Wei Jing

The people kneading dough are hailed as street artists, but I have found many street industrialists on the street. At the entrance of my alley, there are many stalls. First, let's talk about the so-called "cigarette company" without a signboard. That is a beggar-like man, squatting on the ground, rolling cigarettes. He manufactures them with a wooden cigarette rolling machine that is extremely simple and has a belt strung in the middle. He puts tobacco shreds on the belt, and then places cigarette paper with glue on it, then gently pushes it upwards, and a cigarette rolls out. Although this is made by hand, because his technique is skillful, he can manufacture about four hundred cigarettes a day. Although he earns three small coins on each one, the price is still cheaper than ordinary discount cigarettes, so workers and shop assistants living nearby are all his regular customers every day. Every day, four hundred cigarettes, he doesn't need to worry about overproduction at all.

The second one should be the one hanging "Biscuit King" on the stall. However, this biscuit manufacturing is very ridiculous. Although his signboard is the Biscuit King, what he makes and sells, he says himself, is egg slices. But in reality, the raw materials he uses absolutely do not have eggs. What he uses are really sugar and flour for making biscuits, mixed with some water. His manufacturing equipment is two pairs of irons and a charcoal furnace. On the iron, he scoops a spoonful of flour slurry, closes the iron, and puts it on the furnace to bake. Then he starts scooping the slurry onto the second iron. When the second iron is placed on the furnace and the first iron is replaced, the so-called "egg slice" inside has already matured. Making it in this never ending cycle, he can make five or six hundred pieces a day. These five or six hundred pieces are completely sold to the children in the alley. The price is five pennies per piece, and twenty pennies for five pieces. His profit is three pennies on one penny. But if you only buy two pieces from him, he has a profit of four pennies.

There is also a flatbread stall. To put it grandly, it is simply a flatbread company boss for the common people, who has changed to making and selling so-called "hygienic soda" and "hygienic fresh orange juice." His signboard is the three characters "Wang Guangli," but this is irrelevant, because eight or nine out of ten of his customers are illiterate. His hygienic soda is cold boiled water with sugar juice and baking soda. A half-foot-tall bottle, ten pennies for three bottles. Fresh orange juice uses orange juice fruit syrup instead of baking soda, forty pennies per bottle. A thriving career. At the hottest time, he can earn about two thousand pennies a day, because he puts some ice shavings in the hygienic soda and fresh orange juice, so it is very popular with customers.

These, although the scale is so simple that it is not worth mentioning, but calling them street manufacturers, I think it is worthy of the name.

Swapped Mandarin Ducks 188

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Nine: Vowing Hearts in Water and Talking Sadly in Green Lamps, Reporting Lovesickness with Gilded Fingers and Red Beans

Guoqi looked at the letter on the table, neither telling Youmei to take it away, nor stopping her. Youmei slowly walked to the edge of the table, held the small envelope in her hand, gently tossed it up and down, and smiled: I can't guess what's in here. Guoqi smiled: This is nothing more than sending goose feathers from a thousand miles away, the gift is light but the affection is heavy. When Youmei heard this sentence, she saw through his meaning. Looking at the four characters "Forever to be Good" written on the envelope, she smiled and nodded at the paper bag. Guoqi said: This is an idiom I used from the Book of Songs. "He gives me a peach, I give him a jade pendant in return. It is not a return, but forever to be good." Originally, it was a bit incomprehensible for me to quote these words. The gold ring that people sent is a thousand times more valuable than a peach. The two red beans I sent to people are even a thousand times worse than jade. I don't stress the three characters that it is not a return. Youmei ignored this, and smiled: I'll take it away. Guoqi nodded: You're too enthusiastic. Youmei said: Just now my cousin said that he doesn't need this kind of souvenir anymore, I'm a little unconvinced. When I see him later, I'll see if he needs it. Guoqi said: I feel that my treatment of friends is sincere. As for whether friends can understand, I dare not say. Youmei stood still, but leaned half of her body and looked at him, smiling: Cousin, I'm leaving, do you have anything else to say? Guoqi said: I don't have anything to say. Saying these words, he also looked at her. Seeing that the white powder rubbed on her cheeks was already showing moisture, she had been sitting upright for a long time, and she had not prepared a fan for others, and she was a little sweaty. He held the folding fan with both hands, and arched it high: I'm sorry to trouble you. Youmei smiled: Are we still being polite? Cousin! In the sound of her calling him "cousin," she nodded and left in a hurry. When she passed by in front of him, a faint fragrance still fell on her body. Guoqi couldn't help but feel a little about her, feeling that compared to Menglan, they were simply two different people, but she was very willing to help her friends, which was rare. He didn't know if Menglan could help him in this way if she was in this situation. It's just that she is a very quiet person who is shy to see people, so she probably can't be so straightforward and neat. Because of this, he suffered from this point of gentle nature.

Lohan and Bombers 189

During this time of national crisis, all unnecessary construction should be stopped, people believe. For example, the Six Harmonies Pagoda in Hangzhou certainly need not be rebuilt, and even the Leifeng Pagoda need not be planned for reconstruction just because it collapsed.

Now, the Arhat Hall of Lingyin Temple has been carelessly burned down and is about to be rebuilt. It's careless to begin with, and wasteful afterwards, truly pointless.

Indulging in dance halls is surely ignorant of the sorrows of national subjugation, but using precious money to squander on emptiness in these difficult times, what real benefit does it bring to the country? It would be better to buy a bomber for several hundred thousand yuan, to save the people from the great calamity, that would be more charitable. (Lan Ren)

Tiger Fishing 190

— Zhang Feng

Legend has it that a tiger's tail has a fishy smell. When hungry, it dangles its tail by the river to lure fish for food. Unexpectedly, such a large creature, accommodates its hunger with small pickings, sometimes even resulting in death from a small mouth. Near the river mouth at the Yuezhou city wall, a tiger was dangling its tail to lure fish, when a large turtle happened to pass by in the water. Smelling the fishy scent, it suddenly poked its head out of the water and bit the tiger's tail, holding on tightly. The tiger was in great pain and quickly jumped up, accidentally falling into the crenellations of the city wall. The tiger was inside the crenellations, the turtle was outside, looking like a load being carried on a pole. The tiger thrashed its tail even faster in pain, and the turtle bit even tighter in fright. Someone saw it from under the city wall and managed to catch them both. Then, that person slaughtered the tiger but released the turtle into the river, rewarding it for its service in capturing the tiger.

Has Winter Arrived? 191

— Man Ling

The sky is dark and gloomy, and people say, "Winter has arrived."

In the city, the chimneys of furnaces are gradually emerging from the windows of the capitalists, arranged high and low in the pale gray sky. The young ladies go to dance halls, wearing fur coats and high-heeled leather shoes, sitting in streamlined cars, with boyfriends snuggling beside them, the car cutting through the northwest wind, speeding forward. Winter? Is it really winter? The wealthy don't know that winter has arrived!

The northwest wind howls, the heavy snow flies, wearing steel helmets, single-layered shoes, holding guns, dragging cannons, marching forward! Charging! The soldiers fighting bandits on the front lines, only knowing to bring honor to the country and protect the people, how would they know that winter has arrived?

Saving the Nation with Mahjong 192

A friend of mine is fond of gambling, and there isn't a day that he doesn't play mahjong. Since the fake bandits invaded Suiyuan, when the news arrived, the entire nation was filled with indignation. Donations poured in from all over, and emotions were high. My friend was also moved by this. He told me the other day that although he cannot quit gambling immediately, he will use his gambling funds to meet the needs of saving the nation. Every time he gambles, he will extract a portion, several yuan for large games, several jiao for smaller ones, and donate all of this money to relieve Suiyuan. If he does this every day for a month, the amount will be considerable, he said. I heard this and couldn't name it, so I named it to tell gambling addicts that they could imitate him.

In Memory of the Master of the Wusuoxi Studio 193

— Kuang Youhan

It's rare to find kindred spirits in this floating life. I remember discussing poetry under the lamp and critiquing paintings by the window. In the vast world, who truly understood you late in life? Truly beautiful is Jiangnan, I gaze until the clouds and mountains vanish, my nephew has left!

Achievements and failures were ultimately due to food and clothing. The cuckoo cries its heart out, the phoenix's shadow separates and flies away. My unfulfilled hopes, how can I bear to recall them? Surely you are in heaven, do not refuse to let your soul come back along the path of the underworld.

Gender Transformation (Part Two) 194

— Pei Ming

Because these kinds of male-to-female and female-to-male transformations happen so often, the Olympic Committee has often been at a loss when gender issues arise with female athletes in the games; therefore, a new chapter has been drafted, stipulating that in the future, athletes must undergo medical examinations before participating in competitions.

Medical research has found that this kind of gender transformation is related to the adrenal glands. The adrenal glands are about two inches in size, flat and semi-circular, brownish-yellow in color, attached to the upper front surface of the kidneys, without ducts, directly secreting substances into the bloodstream; when they are healthy, they have a very important relationship with sexual development. When they are not healthy, they can change the skin of women into the rough, hairy skin of men, they can also change the gentle female voice into a low and coarse male voice, causing her to dislike men and reverse her love and hate.

If the two adrenal glands of an animal are removed, it will die after forty-eight hours. This proves that the adrenal glands are also essential organs for life.

Ten years ago, a female patient came to Charing Cross Hospital in London. Her symptoms were: facial hair growth, body contours becoming closer to those of a man, such as broad shoulders, and enlarged pelvis; excessive development of bones and muscles; rough skin; deep voice; immature development of sexual organs; underdeveloped breasts; and a change in psychological concept towards men. After abdominal dissection, it was found that one adrenal gland was enlarged. During the first surgery, surgeon and adrenal gland specialist Lennox Ross Broster removed the enlarged adrenal gland, and the hair on the woman's face and arms immediately disappeared, her voice returned to a female tone, and her previously flat breasts became fuller.

This discovery and treatment are all thanks to Dr. Broster, who is still diligently researching this topic. (The End)

World News

The Past and Present of China's Embassy in Japan 195

— Ji Yun

China and Japan are only separated by a narrow strip of water, and their relationship is the closest, so the history of international negotiations between the two countries is also the longest. Recently, with the adjustment of national relations, the platitude of cooperation and friendship has once again been much talked about, and as a result, China's embassy in Japan has been drawing more intense attention.

China's embassy in Japan is located in the Azabu district of Tokyo, near the embassies of Italy and the Soviet Union, which can be said to be the center of Japanese diplomacy. The Qing Dynasty first sent He Ruzhang as the first minister to Japan in the seventh year of the Guangxu reign. Later, the Sino-Japanese War broke out, and the entire embassy lowered its flag and returned to the country. After the establishment of the Republic, Ma Tingliang was appointed minister to Japan in the second year of the Republic. Jiang Zuobin went to Japan as minister to Japan in the nineteenth year of the Republic, and later, in October of last year, Jiang was promoted to ambassador to Japan. Jiang's term has been two or three years, the longest time stationed in Japan. The current Xu Shiying came to Japan in mid-April of this year.

It is difficult to see the Chinese national flag in Japan. Although among the flags of all nations at ordinary gatherings, there is also our Qing Tian Bai Ri Man Di Hong (Blue Sky White Sun Red Earth) flag, not only are the dimensions incorrect, but the number of points may also be wrong. There is a huge party emblem on the iron gate of our embassy, and the three-colored national flag of blue, white, and red flies in the skies of the Japanese empire. Besides the embassy, perhaps only the roof of the Student Supervision Office has the qualification to hang the national flag. In the foreign legation district of Dongjiaomin Lane in Beiping, all foreign embassies have troops stationed there, but outside the gate of our embassy in Japan, there is a Japanese policeman stationed, questioning guests who are visiting the ambassador. It is said that in the past, due to certain reasons, the embassy requested the Japanese Metropolitan Police Department to set up this gate post, and it has been a tradition ever since, and has not yet been removed.

The building of the embassy was originally the villa of Marquis Tokugawa Yorinori, and has now been rebuilt into a two-story Western-style building. Outside is a simple garden, very much like a small rural residence in Europe and America. In the ambassador's reception room upstairs, the decorations are full of Japanese flavor. Several Fujian lacquer vases decorate the room in a very quiet way. On the wall, there are no Chinese paintings or calligraphy, only a huge Xiang embroidery, which is a colorful tiger. I remember that in the past, the French Tiger Prime Minister and our Chinese Little Cat representative became famous stories in the diplomatic world. Indeed, our China now lacks tiger diplomacy to break the international crisis.

During the great earthquake in Japan, many overseas Chinese in Yokohama and Tokyo were killed. At that time, the embassy did not have accurate statistics on overseas Chinese, and it was impossible to investigate for a while. Now, in addition to the students being managed by the Student Supervision Office, the embassy also manages overseas Chinese affairs. Last month, due to national election matters, they were busy investigating the situation of overseas Chinese, which is very different from before. Japanese magazines say that among the eleven embassies of various countries in Japan, the Soviet and Chinese embassies are the most active, which is something only heaven knows.
